It can be made with or without the meatballs\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2029\n|PortionCalories = 253\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 8\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 1 hour 20 minutes\n|PrepTime = 15 minutes\n|CookTime = 1 hour 5 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Ash-e anar (pomegranate soup) recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n======Best recipe review======\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Iranian Soup</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Reminds me of Farhad</span> \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis unusual soup has Persian origins.  It can be made with or without the [[Meatballs|meatballs]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| &#190; cup [[Lentils|lentils]]\n| 3 tablespoons [[Butter|butter]]\n| 1 [[Onion|onion]], peeled and chopped\n| 8 cups water (2 quarts)\n| 1 cup long-[[Grain|grain]] [[Rice|rice]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Turmeric|turmeric]] powder\n| &#189; cup chopped fresh [[Parsley|parsley]]\n| &#189; cup spring [[Onions|onions]], chopped\n| 1 cup [[Pomegranate|pomegranate]] juice or &#189; cup [[Pomegranate syrup|pomegranate syrup]] mixed with &#189; cup water\n| 2 tablespoons chopped fresh [[Mint|mint]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Raisins|raisins]], [[Sultanas|sultanas]] or chopped [[Dried|dried]] [[Apricots|apricots]]\n| 450 g (1 lb) [[Minced|minced]] [[Beef|beef]], shaped into [[Meatballs|meatballs]] (optional)\n| Pinch of sea [[Salt|salt]] and [[Freshly ground pepper|freshly ground pepper]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Wash and drain the [[Lentils|lentils]] after checking for stones etc.\n| Melt 2 tablespoons of [[Butter|butter]] in a large pan and [[Fry|fry]] the [[Onions|onions]] for 5 minutes until softened\n| Add the [[Meatballs|meatballs]], [[Rice|rice]], [[Lentils|lentils]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] and stir [[Fry|fry]] for a minutes or two\n| Add the [[Salt|salt]] and water and bring to the [[Boil|boil]]\n| Reduce the heat, cover and [[Simmer|simmer]] for 40 minutes or until the [[Lentils|lentils]] are cooked\n| Add the [[Pomegranate|pomegranate]] juice and [[Simmer|simmer]] for another 15 minutes\n| Meanwhile, melt the remaining tablespoons of [[Butter|butter]] and [[Sautee|sautee]] the [[Mint|mint]] and [[Raisins|raisins]] for a minute\n| Add to the soup with the chopped spring [[Onions|onions]] and [[Parsley|parsley]]\n| Sprinkle with a few [[Pomegranate|pomegranate]] seeds and serve\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#lentils #pomegranate #onions #butter #asheanar #meatballs #raisins #fry #rice #simmer #parsley </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

-->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 539\n|PortionCalories = 134\n|DatePublished=9th December 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves \ud83d\ude02</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">(almost)</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nAnother lovely [[Aubergine|aubergine]] recipe, this time with [[Pomegranate seeds|pomegranate seeds]].\n\n'''For the [[Saffron|saffron]] [[Yoghurt|yogurt]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| A small pinch of [[Saffron|saffron]]\n| 45ml hot water\n| 180g [[Greek yogurt]]\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, crushed\n| 40ml [[Lime juice|lime juice]]\n| 45ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n}}\n'''For the [[Aubergines|aubergines]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 3 medium [[Aubergines|aubergines]], sliced 2cm thick\n| [[Olive oil]]\n}}\n'''To finish'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 2 tablespoons [[Pine nuts|pine nuts]], [[Toasted|toasted]]\n| The [[Seeds|seeds]] of 1 [[Pomegranate|pomegranate]]\n| 20 [[Basil leaves|basil leaves]] (or [[Dried|dried]] [[Basil|basil]] if fresh unavailable)\n| Seasoning\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to  220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7), [fan oven 200\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n===Method===\n'''For the [[Saffron|saffron]] [[Yoghurt|yogurt]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Infuse the [[Saffron|saffron]] in the hot water for 5 minutes.\n| Pour into a jug with the [[Yoghurt|yogurt]], [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]], [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and a little [[Salt|salt]].\n| Whisk well, adjust seasoning and chill.\n}}\n'''For the [[Aubergines|aubergines]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Place the [[Aubergine|aubergine]] slices on a [[Baking tray|baking tray]] and [[Brush|brush]] them all over with [[Olive oil|olive oil]].\n| Season and [[Bake|bake]] for 35 minutes until golden [[Brown|brown]].\n| Allow to cool.\n}}\n'''To finish'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Arrange the [[Aubergine|aubergine]] slices on a plate, slightly overlapping.\n| Drizzle the [[Yoghurt|yogurt]] over them and sprinkle the [[Pine nuts|pine nuts]], [[Pomegranate seeds|pomegranate seeds]] and [[Basil|basil]] over the top.\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n* Lightly adapted from a recipe in '''Ottolenghi: The Cookbook''' (ISBN 0091922348) by ''Yotam Ottolenghi & Sami Tamimi''\n===Chef's notes===\nThe [[Aubergines|aubergines]] and the [[Yoghurt|yogurt]] mixture will keep separately in the [[Fridge|fridge]] for up to 3 days.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light                         "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Baharat recipe Accompaniments \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#baharat #spice #paprika #spices #nutmeg #cuminseeds #blackpepper #dried #corianderseeds #cinnamon #blackpeppercorns \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Baharat is a spice mixture or blend used throughout the Levant, in Lebanese, Syrian, Jordanian, Iraqi, Libyan and Palestinian cuisine\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 20\n|PortionCalories = 20\n|DatePublished=24th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Baharat in a large airtight container\n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 3\n|TotalTime = 15 minutes\n|PrepTime = 15 minutes\n|CookTime = None\n|Image = [[Image:Baharat.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Lovely warm spice</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.8</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Great for sprinkling on veggies!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n<!-- [[Image:Baharat recipe.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Typical baharat ingredients]] -->\nBah\u0101r\u0101t is a [[Spice|spice]] mixture or blend used throughout the Levant, in Lebanese, Syrian, Jordanian, Iraqi, Libyan and Palestinian cuisine. Baharat, in Arabic, means \"[[Spices|spices]]\". The name originated in Medieval India, as Bh\u0101rat, a Sanskrit name for India, was the source of these [[Spices|spices]]. The mixture of finely [[Ground|ground]] spices is often used to season [[Lamb|lamb]], [[Fish|fish]], [[Chicken|chicken]], [[Beef|beef]], and [[Soups|soups]]. Additionally, it may be used as a [[Condiment|condiment]], to add more flavour after a meal has been prepared.\n\nUnless you are going to use tons of the stuff, assume half or even a quarter of a teaspoon for one part\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 4 parts [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| 3 parts [[Coriander seeds|coriander seeds]]\n| 3 parts [[Cinnamon|cinnamon]]\n| 3 parts [[Cloves|cloves]]\n| 4 parts [[Cumin seeds|cumin seeds]]\n| 1 part [[Cardamom pods|cardamom pods]]\n| 3 parts [[Nutmeg|nutmeg]]\n| 6 parts [[Paprika|paprika]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Grind all of the ingredients to a fine powder in a [[Spice|spice]] mill or [[Coffee grinder|coffee grinder]].\n| [[Dried]] and pulverised [[Kaffir lime leaves|kaffir lime leaves]] can also be added to taste.\n| The mixture can be rubbed into [[Meat|meat]] or mixed with [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and [[Lime juice|lime juice]] to form a [[Marinade|marinade]].\n}}\n\n===Servings===\nServes 20 - Makes a small jar of baharat\n===Variations===\n'''Possible ingredients may be:'''\n[[Allspice]]\n[[Black peppercorns]]\n[[Cardamom seeds]]\n[[Cassia bark]]\n[[Cloves]]\n[[Coriander seeds]]\n[[Cumin seeds]]\n[[Nutmeg]]\n[[Dried red chili peppers]] or [[Paprika|paprika]]\nTurkish baharat includes [[Mint|mint]] as a key ingredient. In Tunisia, bharat refers to a simple mixture of [[Dried|dried]] rosebuds and [[Ground cinnamon|ground cinnamon]], often combined with [[Black pepper|black pepper]]. In the Gulf States, loomi (dried black [[Lime|lime]]) and [[Saffron|saffron]] may also be used for the kebsa [[Spice|spice]] mixture (also called \"Gulf baharat\").\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Lebanese recipes]]\n[[Category:Marinades dressings and butters]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#baharat #spice #paprika #spices #nutmeg #cuminseeds #blackpepper #dried #corianderseeds #cinnamon #blackpeppercorns </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }

title": "Barbecued Harissa lamb",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Barbecued Harissa lamb, Barbecue recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#lamb #barbecuedharissalamb #barbecue #garlic #lemon #harissa #seeds #homemadepittabreads #pestleandmortar #miseenplace #griddled \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A kettle barbecue will give this lamb a deeply smoky flavour, but you can cook it just as well on an open one\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 4952\n|PortionCalories = 825\n|DatePublished=19th August 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Served in a [[homemade pitta bread]] with a salad\n |Servings = Serves 6\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 1 hour\n |PrepTime = 30 minutes\n |CookTime = 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Barbecued Harissa lamb recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">As good as it looks</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">The perfect spicy kebab, made at home.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nA kettle [[Barbecue|barbecue]] will give this [[Lamb|lamb]] a deeply smoky flavour, but you can cook it just as well on an open one.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 tablespoon of [[coriander seeds]] \n| 1 tablespoon of [[cumin seeds]] \n| 3 tablespoons of Belazu Rose [[Harissa]] \n| juice of 1 [[lemon]] \n| Belazu [[extra virgin olive oil]] \n| 3 cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]] \n| 1.6 kg leg of [[lamb]], boned and butterflied (ask your butcher to do this for you)\n| I used a frozen half-leg of lamb and [[butterflied]] it myself.  It was a bit of a fiddle but it worked out fine in the end! \n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 230\u00b0 C (450\u00b0 F - gas 8) if not using a [[Barbecue|barbecue]]\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Marinaded half-leg of lamb cooked.jpg|After 3 hours in the oven\nImage:Marinaded half-leg of lamb.jpg|Marinaded, ready to cook\nImage:Butterflied half-leg of lamb.jpg|A poorly butterflied leg of lamb\nImage:Half-leg of lamb.jpg|Half-leg of (frozen) lamb, defrosted<br />[\u00a36.50 Morrisons - August 2013]\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Put the [[Seeds|seeds]] in a [[Pestle and mortar|pestle and mortar]] and crush slightly. \n| Mix the [[Harissa]], [[Lemon|lemon]], 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Spices|spices]] together, smear over the [[Lamb|lamb]]\n| [[Marinate|marinate]] for at least one hour. \n| Season well and cook on a heated [[Barbecue|barbecue]] with the lid on for 25-30 minutes, turning a couple of times. \n| Allow to rest for 10 minutes before carving.\n}}\n(''[[Olive]] magazine'')\n\n===Serving suggestion===\nServe in [[homemade pitta breads]] with a selection of chopped salad vegetables.\n\n===Chef's notes===\nWhen preparing this dish, the decision to barbecue or not was weather dependant, in the end I decided not to barbecue.  After butterflying the half-leg of lamb, and seeing how cartilaginous and sinewy the meat was, I thought slow cooking would give a far better result than cooking quickly in the oven or even barbecuing.  This was a great decision as the resulting meat just fell apart, juicy and tender.\n\nI placed marinated meat on an uncovered grill tray at the top of the highest setting on my oven (260\u00b0C [500\u00b0F) Gas 10]\tand left for 15 minutes, then I reduced the oven to 180\u00b0C [350\u00b0F - Gas 4] placed meat in an oven tray covered in tin-foil and cooked for another 2.5 hours.  It looks burnt from the picture, but if you look at the kebab in the pitta you'll see how tender it was - with no gristle.\n\n{{Template:Belazu attribution}}\n===Belazu products used in this recipe===\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/products/extra virgin-olive-oils.html Belazu Extra virgin olive oil]\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/rose-harissa.html Belazu Rose Harissa]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Barbecue recipes]]\n[[Category:Belazu recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n[[Category:Lamb recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Mutton recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:Moroccan recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#lamb #barbecuedharissalamb #barbecue #garlic #lemon #harissa #seeds #homemadepittabreads #pestleandmortar #miseenplace #griddled </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }

title": "Basbousa",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Basbousa, Greek recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#basbousa #semolina #butter #honey #bakingpowder #bakingsoda #boil #cream #almond #bake #bakingtray \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Basbousa, basboosa,(Arabic), ravani (Turkish) or revani (Greek \u03c1\u03b1\u03b2\u03b1\u03bd\u03b9 and \u03c1\u03b5\u03b2\u03b1\u03bd\u03b9) is a sweet cake made of a semolina soaked in syrup\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 3681\n|PortionCalories = 245\n|DatePublished=27th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 15 - Makes 1 cake\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour\n |PrepTime = 20 minutes\n |CookTime = 40 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Basbousa recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Kate Bush song, shurely?</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">So this is what she was singing about, it must be good \ud83e\udd13</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Sue_spins|Susie]] </span></span>\n}}\n\n'''Basbousa''', '''basboosa''',(Arabic), '''ravani''' (Turkish) or '''revani''' (Greek \u03c1\u03b1\u03b2\u03b1\u03bd\u03af and \u03c1\u03b5\u03b2\u03b1\u03bd\u03af) is a sweet cake made of a [[Semolina|semolina]] soaked in syrup. [[Coconut]] is a popular addition to the cake. Although Greeks of Southern Greeks call it '''ravani''', in the north it is called '''revani''', as in Turkish, specifically in the town of Veria where it has been the traditional dessert for many years.\n\nIt is found in the cuisines of the eastern Mediterranean under a variety of names. It appears to be a variant of the Egyptian dish '''ma'mounia'''. Basbousa is very common is Arabia.\n\nBasbousa is routinely called \"'''Hareesa'''\" in arabic countries such as Palestine. It is said to have originated as Hareesa before subsequent movements by other countries (such as Iraq, Turkey, and Libya) who shifted the name to Basbousa.\n\nThere are many varieties, of which this is just one!\n\n\n'''Syrup'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2.25 cups [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| 1.5 cups water\n| [[Juice]] of 1 [[Lemon|lemon]] (or 2 tablespoons [[Orange juice|orange juice]])\n| 1 teaspoon [[Honey|honey]]\n}}\n'''Cake'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 2 cups [[Semolina|semolina]]\n| 1 cup [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| 113 g (4 oz) [[Butter|butter]], softened\n| 1 cup whole [[Milk|milk]]\n| 1.5 teaspoons [[Vanilla extract|vanilla extract]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Baking powder|baking powder]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Baking soda|baking soda]]\n| 2 [[free range eggs]]\n| [[Blanched]] split [[Almonds|almonds]] to garnish\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4)\n===Method===\n'''Syrup'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a medium saucepan, dissolve the [[Sugar|sugar]] in water.\n| Add the [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] and bring to a [[Boil|boil]].\n| Once the syrup starts to [[Boil|boil]], stir in the [[Honey|honey]].\n| Reduce the heat and allow [[Simmer|simmer]]  for about 8-10 minutes.\n| Remove from heat and set aside.\n}}\n'''Cake'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Lightly grease and [[Flour|flour]] a 23 cm x 30 cm (9\"x12\") [[baking tray]].\n| [[Cream]] the [[Butter|butter]] and [[Sugar|sugar]] in a mixing bowl.\n| Add the [[Eggs|eggs]] and stir in the [[vanilla]].\n| In a separate bowl, combine [[Semolina|semolina]], [[Baking powder|baking powder]], and [[Baking soda|baking soda]].\n| Slowly add to [[Butter|butter]] and [[Egg|egg]] mixture and then stir in the [[Milk|milk]].\n| Pour the mixture into [[Baking|baking]] dish and smooth with a spatula.\n| Take a knife and scribe a diamond pattern in the top and place an [[Almond|almond]] in the centre of each diamond. [[Bake]] for 25 minutes.\n| Remove cake from [[Oven|oven]] and the pour syrup over the cake until no more can be absorbed.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nAllow to cool for 20 minutes before serving.\n\nServe with [[Cinnamon ice-cream|cinnamon ice-cream]]\n===Variations===\nA little [[Rose water|rose water]] can be added in place of the water.\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Greek recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Sweets and desserts]]\n[[Category:Turkish recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#basbousa #semolina #butter #honey #bakingpowder #bakingsoda #boil #cream #almond #bake #bakingtray </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }
}

title": "Beetroot falafel with toasted halloumi cheese",
                "revisions": [

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Beetroot falafel with toasted halloumi cheese recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#beetrootfalafelwithtoastedhalloumicheese #tahini #oliveoil #yogurt #coffeegrinder #mortarandpestle #toasted #beetroot #falafel #breadcrumbs #dip \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This vegetarian salad make a visually exciting meal that is also healthy. The salty toasted halloumi cheese compliments the sweet falafel\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 4440\n|PortionCalories = 740\n|DatePublished=13th August 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 6\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour 10 minutes\n|PrepTime =  40 minutes\n|CookTime =  30 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Beetroot falafel with toasted halloumi cheese recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Perfect veggie meal</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Just made this again for some vegetarian friends who thought it was fabulous!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis [[Vegetarian|vegetarian]] [[Salad|salad]] make a visually exciting meal that is also healthy.  The salty  [[Toasted|toasted]] [[Halloumi cheese|halloumi cheese]] compliments the sweet [[Falafel|falafel]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| [[Olive oil]]\n| 1 x 250 g pack of [[Halloumi cheese|halloumi cheese]]\n| 1 medium [[Onions|onion]], peeled and sliced\n| 2 teaspoons [[Cumin seeds|cumin seeds]], ground to a fine powder [[coffee grinder]] or a [[Mortar and pestle|mortar and pestle]]\n| 1 teaspoon of [[coriander seeds]], ground to a fine powder [[coffee grinder]] or a [[Mortar and pestle|mortar and pestle]]\n| 1 teaspoon of [[fenugreek seeds]], ground to a fine powder [[coffee grinder]] or a [[Mortar and pestle|mortar and pestle]]\n| 1 teaspoon of [[chilli powder]]\n| 1 tablespoon of freshly chopped [[parsley]]\n| 1 [[Free range egg|free range egg]]\n| 300 g (10.5 oz) pre cooked (but not pickled) [[Beetroot|beetroot]]. Trimmed, peeled and very roughly chopped\n| 100g (4 oz) [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]]\n| 2 x 400g cans of [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]] drain and rinsed well under cold running water\n| 1 tablespoon light [[Tahini|tahini]]\n| [[Salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n'''to serve'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 300 ml [[Yogurt|yogurt]]\n| 1 tablespoon light [[Tahini|tahini]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Add a tablespoon or so of the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] to a [[Frying pan|frying pan]] and give it a good twist of [[Black pepper|black pepper]].\n| Saut\u00e9 the [[Onions|onions]] over a low heat for about 5 minutes - don't [[Brown|brown]] them.\n| Add the [[Cumin seeds|cumin seeds]] and [[Fry|fry]] for a further minute or so.\n| Allow to cool for a few minutes then add to a [[Food processor|food processor]] with a metal blade.  Don't run until all of the ingredients have been added\n| Add to this; the [[Beetroot|beetroot]], [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]], 1 tablespoon of [[Tahini|tahini]], the [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]] and the [[Egg|egg]].\n| Blitz to a rough consistency, don't over-[[Blend|blend]]. Aim for some texture, not babyfood.\n| Ideally, leave the mixture to rest for 30 minutes or more before cooking to allow the breadcrumbs to rehydrate a little\n| Using you hands, form into about 20 golf-ball sized balls and them flatten into patties.  A great tip from Jamie Oliver's 15 minutes meals, when moulding [[falafel]]s is to wet your hands first.  This prevents the gooey mixture from sticking to your hands.\n| Gently [[shallow fry]] for 15 to 20 minutes until crusted and caramelised on the outside.  \n| Meanwhile, slice the [[Halloumi|halloumi]] width-wise into about 10 slices, [[Spray|spray]] with [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and [[Griddle|griddle]] until nicely [[Toasted|toasted]] - it won't melt.\n| Mix a tablespoon or so of the [[Tahini|tahini]] into the [[Yogurt|yogurt]], season and mix well to serve as a [[Dip|dip]].\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Beetroot falafel balls.jpg|Half to cook now, half to freeze\nImage:Beetroot falafel with toasted halloumi cheese_ingredients.jpg|Beetroot falafel mixture, ready to rest\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe on a bed of [[Green salad|green salad]] with the [[Toasted|toasted]] [[Halloumi|halloumi]], the [[Yogurt|yogurt]] [[Dip|dip]] and warm [[Pitta breads|pitta breads]].\n===Variations===\nThese could also be [[oven baked]] or [[Deep-fried|deep-fried]] until crisped on the outside.\n\nThese could be shaped into balls, laid out on [[greaseproof paper]] over a baking tray, placed in the [[freezer]] then bagged up once completely frozen for later use.  I would be inclined to allow them to completely defrost before cooking, especially if you were to fry them.\n===Chef's notes===\nI did make these with whole spices, but the effect was rather bland so have amended to finely ground spices which should 'spread' the flavour further.\n\nThe falafel pictured were oven baked.  Next time I would flatten them and shallow fry them so the outsides caramelise.  This did not happen with oven baking.\n\nOven directions: Heat [[Oven|oven]] to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6), [fan oven 180\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour], spread out on a baking tray and spray or brush with [[olive oil]] before baking for 3 minutes.\n{{SeeAlso-HalloumiRecipes}}\n* [[Beetroot recipes|Our favourite beetroot recipes]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Greek recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Tunisian recipes]]\n[[Category:Turkish recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#beetrootfalafelwithtoastedhalloumicheese #tahini #oliveoil #yogurt #coffeegrinder #mortarandpestle #toasted #beetroot #falafel #breadcrumbs #dip </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Belazu Chicken Couscous",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Belazu Chicken Couscous, Meat recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#belazuchickencouscous #couscous #arganoil #ginger #chicken #onion #saffron #harissapaste #wok #bouquetgarni #herb \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is a great recipe for you to try out your argan oil\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2795\n|PortionCalories = 465\n|DatePublished=28th July 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 6\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 45 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Belazu Chicken Couscous recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Lovely harissa</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Harissa paste makes the difference. To be honest, I could not tell if the argan oil made it taste any different.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Belazu Chicken Couscous simmer.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Chicken ready to simmer]]\nThis is a great recipe for you to try out your [[argan oil]].  It's also a nice way to cook chicken.\n\nTraditional [[Harissa paste|harissa paste]] really [[Spices|spices]] up the [[Couscous|couscous]].\n\nTo serve less, use the same amount of rub and herbs, just cover with less stock.  One chicken leg per person is ample.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1.3 kg [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces (6 chicken legs) \n| 1 teaspoon [[Ground|ground]] [[Ginger|ginger]] \n| 1 teaspoon [[Black pepper|black pepper]] \n| 1 teaspoon [[Salt|salt]] \n| 1 sachet [[Saffron|saffron]] filaments \n| 4 tablespoons of [[Belazu]] [[Argan oil]] \n| 1 [[Onion|onion]], peeled and sliced\n| 200 ml [[Chicken stock]] or [[vegetable stock]] to cover the chicken pieces.\n| Big sprig of your choice of herbs - [[Bouquet garni|a good list of suggestions here]]\n| 120 g [[couscous]] (''Follow the link for cooking instructions'')\n}}\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Put the [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces in a bowl with the [[Ginger|ginger]], [[Pepper|pepper]], [[Salt|salt]] and [[Saffron|saffron]]. Rub these in using your hands.\n|[[Brown|brown]] in a [[wok]] or [[Casserole dish|casserole dish]] with the [[argan oil]].\n| Add the sliced [[Onion|onion]], and soften for 2-3 minutes, then top up with enough stock to just cover the chicken pieces.\n| Make a [[Herb|herb]] bundle by tying the herb sprigs together with [[kitchen string]] and add to the [[wok]] or [[Casserole|casserole]]. | Bring to the [[Boil|boil]] then reduce to a [[Simmer|simmer]] for 30 minutes or until cooked.\n| Remove the cooked chicken and serve, discarding the stock and herbs.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with  [[Harissa paste|harissa paste]] and [[Barley|barley]] [[Couscous|couscous]] or normal couscous.\n===Chef's notes===\nThe original recipe did not specify the cuts of chicken to use, but in this type of dish the flavour is much improved by using cuts that include the bone rather than fillets.  I would skin them first though so the end result is not too greasy.\n\nHalf a [[green pepper]] was chopped and added to the [[couscous]] together with some dried fruit that had been soaked in sherry for 30 minutes.  The rest of the pepper was added to the chicken casserole and discarded once the chicken was cooked.\n\nI used [[fennel]], [[parsley]], [[mint]] and a small amount of [[rosemary]] in my [[bouquet garni]].\n{{Template:Belazu attribution}}\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/argan-oil.html Belazu Argan Oil]\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/rose-harissa.html Belazu Rose Harissa]\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/traditional-barley-couscous.html Belazu Traditional Barley Couscous]\n==See also==\n* {{See also - Jointing a chicken}}\n{{Template:PeelingGinger}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Belazu recipes|Chicken couscous]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes|Chicken couscous]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Chicken couscous]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Chicken couscous]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes|Chicken couscous]]\n[[Category:Moroccan recipes|Chicken couscous]]\n[[Category:North African recipes|Chicken couscous]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes|Chicken couscous]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Chicken couscous]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles|Chicken couscous]]\n[[Category:Tunisian recipes|Chicken couscous]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#belazuchickencouscous #couscous #arganoil #ginger #chicken #onion #saffron #harissapaste #wok #bouquetgarni #herb </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

            }

Remove from the pan immediately. Season, cover and bring to the [[Boil|boil]].\n| Turn down the heat and [[Simmer|simmer]], covered, for 10-15 mins until the [[Beans|beans]] are tender. (Less for [[defrosted]] [[Frozen|frozen]] [[Beans|beans]]). If necessary, top up the water.\n| Add the [[Coriander|coriander]], [[Preserved lemon|preserved lemon]] and [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]], then adjust the seasoning.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe hot or warm with [[Couscous|couscous]] and [[Griddled|griddled]] [[Lamb|lamb]] or river [[Trout|trout]].\n===Variations===\nTry this with other beans or even peas. [[French beans]] would be nice though you would probably want to reduce the cooking time a little.\n(''Good Housekeeping'')\n\n{{Template:Belazu attribution}}\n===Belazu products used in this recipe===\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/products/extra virgin-olive-oils.html Belazu Extra virgin olive oil]\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/belazu-pickled-lemons.html Belazu Preserved Lemon]\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Belazu recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:Moroccan recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tunisian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#broadbeanswithpreservedlemon #beans #broadbeans #belazu #frozen #onion #defrosted #cuminseeds #coriander #preservedlemon #simmer </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

I prefer this cold or at room temperature though but just serve it directly if you want it hot.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 teaspoon [[Vegetable|vegetable]] [[Bouillon|bouillon]] powder or &#189; [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]] cube\n| 120 g dried [[couscous]]\n| Splash of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 2 Small [[Sweet peppers|sweet peppers]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Dry sherry|dry sherry]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Raisins|raisins]] or [[Sultanas|sultanas]]\n| 5 [[Dried apricots|dried apricots]]\n| &#189; a small head of [[Broccoli|broccoli]]\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Almond flakes|almond flakes]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Chop the [[Dried fruit|dried fruit]], place in a saucer and pour over the [[Sherry|sherry]].  Leave for as long as you can so the [[Fruit|fruit]] soaks up the sherry.\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Using [[Boiling|boiling]] water, make up 1.5 x the volume of the [[Couscous|couscous]] (1.5 cups of [[Stock|stock]] to 1 cup of couscous)\n| Add the [[Couscous|couscous]] to a bowl and pour over the [[Stock|stock]].  Mix well and leave until the water is absorbed, about 10 minutes.\n| [[Boil]] or [[Steam|steam]] the [[Broccoli|broccoli]] so it is to your liking.  Chop into small pieces.\n| [[Roast]] the [[Peppers|peppers]], remove the [[Seeds|seeds]] and membrane and chop into small pieces.\n| Toast the [[Almond flakes|almond flakes]] until [[Browned|browned]], be careful not to burn them as they turn very [[Bitter|bitter]] when burnt.\n| Pour the [[Dried fruit|dried fruit]] and any remaining [[Sherry|sherry]] over the [[Couscous|couscous]], add a splash of [[Olive oil|olive oil]], stir in the [[Broccoli|broccoli]] and [[Sweet peppers|sweet peppers]], garnish with the [[Toasted|toasted]] [[Almonds|almonds]] and serve.\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#couscous #broccoli #broccolicouscous #sherry #stock #oliveoil #sweetpeppers #almondflakes #driedfruit #sultanas #boil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Chakchouka (Eggs, tomatoes and chillies)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Chakchouka (Eggs, tomatoes and chillies) an egg recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#eggs #chillies #onion #oliveoil #tomatoes #tomato #garlic #pittabread #sweetpeppers #fry #hilba \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A Libyan breakfast recipe. Variations of this dish are also popular in Algeria and Tunisia\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 442\n|PortionCalories = 110\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 25 minutes\n |PrepTime = 5 minutes\n |CookTime = 20 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Shakshouka.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">A cracking breakfast</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Just the way for a chili-head to start their day!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Sue_spins|Susie]] </span></span>\n}}\nA Libyan breakfast recipe aka ''Shakshuka''.  Variations of this dish are also popular in Algeria and Tunisia.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| [[Olive oil]] for [[Frying|frying]]\n| [[Garlic]] cloves, to taste, chopped\n| 1 [[Onion|onion]], chopped\n| [[Green chillies]], to taste, finely chopped\n| 5 ripe [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], sliced\n| Seasoning\n| 4 large [[Eggs|eggs]]\n}}\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] in a [[Frying pan|frying pan]] and gently [[Fry|fry]] the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Onion|onion]] until soft and golden [[Brown|brown]] (about 10 minutes). \n| Mix in the [[Chillies|chillies]] then arrange the [[Tomato|tomato]] slices on top. \n| Season, then cover and [[Simmer|simmer]] gently for about 15 minutes.\n| Break the [[Eggs|eggs]] into the pan and, using a fork, spread the whites to cover the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]. \n| Cover and cook for about 6 minutes, or until the [[Eggs|eggs]] are done.\n| Cut the mixture into quarters and scoop these out onto warmed serving plates.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Pitta bread|pitta bread]].\n===Variations===\nAdd a little [[Tomato|tomato]] pur\u00e9e to the mixture with the [[Chillies|chillies]] for additional colour or try adding a teaspoon of [[Hilba|hilba]] to it. You can also include [[sweet peppers]].  In North Africa [[merguez]] is sometimes added.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Chakchouka (eggs, tomatoes and chillies)]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes|Chakchouka (eggs, tomatoes and chillies)]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes|Chakchouka (eggs, tomatoes and chillies)]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes|Chakchouka (eggs, tomatoes and chillies)]]\n[[Category:Libyan recipes|Chakchouka (eggs, tomatoes and chillies)]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes|Chakchouka (eggs, tomatoes and chillies)]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Chakchouka (eggs, tomatoes and chillies)]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Chakchouka (eggs, tomatoes and chillies)]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Chakchouka (eggs, tomatoes and chillies)]]\n[[Category:Breakfast recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#eggs #chillies #onion #oliveoil #tomatoes #tomato #garlic #pittabread #sweetpeppers #fry #hilba </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

course, 4 if serving as a snack, accompaniment or first course\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour\n|PrepTime =  20 minutes\n|CookTime =  40 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Chermoula aubergine recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Vegetarian delight!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Tasted as good as yours looked Julia.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\nIf you don't like [[Aubergines|aubergines]], you will change your mind if you try this\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, crushed\n| 2 teaspoons [[Ground cumin|ground cumin]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Ground coriander|ground coriander]]\n| 1 teaspoon extra hot [[Chilli flakes|chilli flakes]]\n| 1 teaspoon hot [[Smoked paprika|smoked paprika]]\n| The finely chopped skin of a small [[Preserved lemon|preserved lemon]] (a [[Belazu]] one is ideal)\n| 140ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]], plus extra\n| 2 medium [[Aubergines|aubergines]]\n| 150g fine [[Bulgur wheat|bulgur wheat]], soaked in 140ml [[Boiling|boiling]] water\n| 50g [[Sultanas|sultanas]], soaked for 10 minutes in warm water\n| 20g fresh [[Coriander|coriander]], finely chopped\n| 50g pitted [[Green olives|green olives]], chopped\n| 30g flaked [[Almonds|almonds]], [[Toasted|toasted]]\n| 3 [[Spring onions|spring onions]], finely chopped\n| 1&frac12; tablespoons [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]]\n| 120ml [[Greek yogurt]]\n| [[Salt]]\n| Fresh [[Parsley|parsley]], chopped, to garnish\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6), [fan oven 180\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n}}\n'''For the [[Chermoula|chermoula]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Mix the [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Cumin|cumin]], [[Coriander|coriander]], [[Chilli|chilli]], [[Paprika|paprika]], [[Preserved lemon|preserved lemon]], 90ml of the [[Oil|oil]] and &frac12; teaspoon [[Salt|salt]] and reserve.\n}}\n'''For the [[Aubergines|aubergines]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Cut them in half lengthways.\n| Cut through the flesh in a criss-cross, ensuring that you don't cut the skin.\n| Spread the [[Chermoula|chermoula]] over the [[Aubergines|aubergines]] and place on a [[Baking tray|baking tray]], cut side up.\n| [[Bake]] for 40 minutes or until the flesh is soft.\n}}\n'''For the topping'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Whilst the [[Aubergines|aubergines]] are [[Baking|baking]], mix the [[Bulgur|bulgur]] with the [[Sultanas|sultanas]], the remaining 50ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]], [[Herbs|herbs]], [[Olives|olives]], [[Almonds|almonds]], [[Spring onions|spring onions]], [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] and a pinch of [[Salt|salt]].\n| Check [[Salt|salt]] and add more if necessary.\n}}\n'''To finish'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Place the [[Aubergines|aubergines]] on plates and spoon the [[Bulgur|bulgur]] mixture on top, allowing some to fall down the sides.\n| Spoon over the [[Yoghurt|yogurt]], sprinkle with chopped [[Parsley|parsley]] and drizzle with a little [[Oil|oil]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe warm or at room temperature.\n===Recipe source===\n\n* Lightly adapted from a recipe in '''Jerusalem''' (ISBN 0091943744) by ''Yotam Ottolenghi and Sami Tamimi''\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Aubergine 358\n|DatePublished=23rd June 2014\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 6\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 1 day, 8 hours\n|PrepTime = 1 day\n|CookTime = 8 hours\n|Image = [[Image:Chicken k'dra with Chickpeas, red peppers and raisins recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span chicken.jpg|thumb|300px|right|A whole turkey leg [1400g] instead of a small chicken]]\nTypical of a lot of [[North African]] recipes, this is a fruity and spicy dish with lots of [[Onions|onions]], but not necessarily hot.\n\nIf you don't have a [[Slow cooker|slow cooker]], [[Chicken kadra with Chickpeas, red peppers and raisins|we have a cooker top version of the same recipe]].\n\nUnless you are using canned [[Chick-peas|chick-peas]], you will need to soak the [[Chick peas|chick peas]] overnight.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 1 [[Chicken|chicken]] cut into about 6 pieces, [[Jointing a chicken|it's very easy to do, see here]]\n| 175g of [[Dried|dried]] [[Chick peas|chick peas]], soaked overnight in cold water, well rinsed and drained\n| 6 medium [[Onions|onions]], peeled and chopped.  About 450g when chopped.  A [[food processor]] is ideal for this task!\n| 2 pinches of [[Saffron|saffron]]\n| 2 [[Cinnamon sticks|cinnamon sticks]]\n| 1 fresh [[bay leaf]]\n| A pinch of [[mixed herbs]]\n| A pinch of [[chilli flakes]]\n| Half a teaspoon of [[chilli flakes]]\n| 850 ml (1.5 pints) of [[Chicken stock]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Smen|smen]] or [[Ghee|ghee]]\n| 2 [[sweet peppers|red peppers]], [[Roasted sweet peppers| roasted, deseeded and slices, see here]]\n| Half a 1 teaspoon [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| 4 tablespoons of chopped [[Dried fruit|dried fruit]] ; [[Raisins|raisins]], [[Sultanas|sultanas]], [[Apricots|apricots]], [[Prunes|prunes]]\n}}\n''' to serve'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| lots of freshly chopped [[Parsley|parsley]]\n| [[Toasted]] [[Almond flakes|almond flakes]]\n| [[Lemon]] wedges\n| Crusty [[Bread|bread]], [[boiled potatoes]] or buttery [[Cous-cous|cous-cous]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* [[Roasted sweet peppers|Roast, skin and deseed]] the [[Red peppers|red peppers]] and slice thinly\n* Separate the [[Chicken|chicken]] into 6 pieces, discard the skin\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| To the [[Slow cooker|slow cooker]], add the [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces, the soaked and drained [[Chick peas|chick peas]], half of the chopped [[Onions|onions]], the [[Saffron strands|saffron strands]], [[Cinnamon sticks|cinnamon sticks]], [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]], [[mixed herbs]], [[turmeric]] and [[chilli flakes]].\n| Add the [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]]\n| Stir well and cook, covered for a 8 hours on low.\n| When there is a few hours left, add the remaining [[Onions|onions]], [[Dried fruit|dried fruit]], [[Smen|smen]] or [[Ghee|ghee]] together with half of the chopped [[Parsley|parsley]] and half of the [[Red pepper|sweet pepper]] slices.\n| Cook for a further 2 hours.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe, scattered with the [[Toasted|toasted]] [[Almonds|almonds]] and the remaining [[Parsley|parsley]] and [[Red pepper|red pepper]] slices.  Accompany with the [[Lemon wedges|lemon wedges]].\n\nThis goes well [[boiled potatoes]], crusty [[Bread|bread]] or buttery [[Cous-cous|cous-cous]]\n===Chef's notes===\nThe cost of a whole chicken from Morrisons was nine pounds which seems ridiculous for a supermarket chicken [June 2014].  Next to the chickens was a huge whole turkey leg (in two pieces), weighing in at 1.4 kg.  For less than half the price of a [[chicken]].  \n\nUsing the whole [[turkey]] leg, I amended the recipe slightly to my personal tastes. I also added a [[bay leaf]], half a teaspoon of [[turmeric]], a pinch of [[mixed herbs]] and some [[chilli flakes]] at the start, and reduced the [[ground pepper]] to just a good pinch.  I've skinned the legs and cut 6 deep slashes right down to the bone so they cook evenly.  I added 700ml (1.5 pints) of chicken stock, which did not cover the turkey legs, but they will still cook perfectly well, especially if you turn them at the final hour.  ''I've [[Roasting a chicken in a slow cooker|roasted a whole chicken in a slow cooker]] and it was perfectly cooked (8 hours on low).''   \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:Moroccan recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Tunisian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted]]\n[[Category:Slow cooked]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Slow cooker recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chicken #onions #chilliflakes #mixedherbs #chickpeas #parsley #smen #chickenstock #slowcooker #turmeric #boiledpotatoes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Cover with water and cook, covered, for 45 minutes to 1 hour until the [[Meat|meat]] is very tender and properly cooked, adding water to keep it covered in its [[Sauce|sauce]]. \n| Add the [[Peas|peas]], [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Preserved lemon|preserved lemon]] and [[Olives|olives]] and cook uncovered a few minutes longer, until the peas are tender and the [[Sauce|sauce]] reduced. These take a while to prepare but are most definitely worth the effort.  Whatever else you put on the kebab sticks is up to your personal taste.\n\nWe've chosen [[Sweet peppers|sweet peppers]] and [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]].\n\nAs I've recently bought a selection of Mae Ploy [[Curry|curry]] pastes, I've used the Mae Ploy [[Massaman curry]] paste in this recipe.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n}}\n====kebabs====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| One massive [[Chicken breast|chicken breast]] fillet\n| Two [[Sweet peppers|sweet peppers]], any colour\n| 24 [[Button mushrooms|button mushrooms]]\n}}\n====marinade====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 4 [[Cloves of Garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves of garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| 250g [[Greek yogurt]]\n| 2 teaspoons Mae Play [[Massaman curry]] paste\n| 1 teaspoon soft [[Brown sugar|brown sugar]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Lime juice|lime juice]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n}}\n====marinade====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Mix all of the [[Marinade|marinade]] ingredients together in a [[Lock & Lock box]] and stir really well to ensure they are properly mixed\n| Cut the [[Chicken|chicken]] into bite-sized pieces and add to the [[Marinade|marinade]]\n| Cover and shake hard so the [[Chicken|chicken]] is evenly coated\n| Leave to [[Marinade|marinade]] for about 5 hours, shaking now and then if you can\n}}\n====kebabs====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| While you assemble the [[Kebabs|kebabs]], preheat you [[Grill|grill]] to maximum\n| Deseed the [[Peppers|peppers]] and cut into squares so they 'fit' the [[Kebabs|kebabs]]\n| Slide the [[Chicken|chicken]], [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] slices onto your [[Kebab|kebab]] sticks - metal [[Skewers|skewers]] work well for us\n| Arrange over a [[Foil|foil]]-lined [[Oven tray|oven tray]] and coat with any spare [[Marinade|marinade]]\n| [[Grill]] for 15 minutes, turning once\n| [[Rest for]] 5 minutes before serving\n}}\n\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Vegetable|vegetable]] [[Rice|rice]] or [[Pittas|pittas]] and a [[Salad|salad]]\n===Variations===\n[[Cherry tomatoes]], slices of [[Fruit|fruit]] and slices of [[Red onion|red onion]] and [[Olives|olives]] go well on these [[Kebabs|kebabs]].\n===Chef's notes===\nThese would be perfect for a [[Barbecue|barbecue]] too, though not for us as it's snowing at the moment!\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Greek recipes]]\n[[Category:Indian recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Thai recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Marinades dressings and butters]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Barbecue recipes]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n[[Category:Marinaded]]\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:12032020'>#marinade #chicken #kebabs #massamancurry #sweetpeppers #chickentikkakebabs #grill #mushrooms #rice #limejuice #olives</code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Add a little [[plain flour]] to thicken if needed. \n| Serve sprinkled with [[parsley]]\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Chicken with Preserved Lemon and Olives browned.jpg|thumb|300px|right|After browning\nImage:Chicken with Preserved Lemon and Olives first cook.jpg|thumb|300px|right|After cooking on the vegetables\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe the [[Chicken|chicken]] on a bed of [[Barley]] [[Couscous|couscous]], with the [[Sauce|sauce]] spooned over.\n\n{{Template:Belazu attribution}}\n===Belazu products used in this recipe===\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/early-harvest.html Belazu Early Harvest Extra Virgin Olive Oil Unfiltered]\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/products/extra virgin-olive-oils.html Belazu Extra virgin olive oil]\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/belazu-pickled-lemons.html Belazu Preserved Lemon]\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/traditional-barley-couscous.html Belazu Traditional Barley Couscous]\n\n==See also==\n* {{See also - Jointing a chicken}}\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Belazu recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chickenwithpreservedlemonandolives #chicken #preservedlemon #couscous #wine #garlic #oliveoil #belazu #barley #casserole #redonions </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

It's sort of like a chunky hummus\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2537\n|PortionCalories = 634\n|DatePublished=13th November 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 1 day, 45 minutes\n|PrepTime = 1 day\n|CookTime =  45 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Chickpea salad with red onions goats cheese and paprika recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Vegetarian loviliness</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.67</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Visually exciting and very tasty.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Chickpea salad with red onions goats cheese vacuum packed.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Left-overs [[vacuum packed]] and ready to freeze]]\nStandard Moroccan fare, this [[Vegetarian|vegetarian]] [[Main course|main course]] is delicious served with [[Home-made pitta bread|homemade pitta bread]].  It's sort of like a chunky [[hummus]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 225 g of [[Dried|dried]] [[Chick peas|chick peas]] soaked overnight in cold water - 2 drained 400g cans of tinned [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]] is an equivalent amount\n| 1 large [[Red onion|red onion]], peeled and sliced into thin strips\n| 1 teaspoon freshly [[Ground cumin seeds|ground cumin seeds]]\n| Half a teaspoon of dried [[oregano]]\n| 4 large [[Cloves of Garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves of garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| 2 teaspoons of [[Smoked paprika powder|smoked paprika powder]]\n| 3 tablespoons of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] plus a little extra\n| [[Juice]] and [[Zest|zest]] from 1 fresh [[Lime|lime]]\n| Bunch of fresh [[Parsley leaves|parsley leaves]], washed and finely chopped\n| Bunch of fresh [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]], washed and finely chopped\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n''' to serve'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 125g [[Goats' cheese|goats' cheese]], crumbled\n| 6 [[Home-made pitta breads]]\n\n}}\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| If using dried [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]], drain and rinse well, place in a heave saucepan covered with cold water, bring to the [[Boil|boil]] and [[Simmer|simmer]] for 45 minutes.  Drain the [[Boiled|boiled]] [[Peas|peas]] and remove and discard any loose skins.\n| If using canned [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]], just rinse and drain well, they are already cooked.\n| Add the [[Olive oil|olive oil]], [[black pepper]], [[Garlic|garlic]], sliced [[Onions|onions]] to a [[Wok|wok]] or large [[Frying pan|frying pan]] and saut\u00e9 for 5 minutes, just enough to take the edge off the [[Garlic|garlic]] and to caramelise the [[Onions|onions]] a little.\n| Tip in the [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]], [[Paprika|paprika]], [[Ground cumin|ground cumin]], [[Salt|salt]], [[Lime juice|lime juice]] and [[Zest|zest]] together with the [[Herbs|herbs]] and toss well so everything is coated.\n|If you make this ahead of time I would make it without the fresh herbs, [[lime zest]] and [[lime|juice]] but add any extra [[olive oil]], leaving it in the pan or wok for the flavours to amalgamate.  Reheat the pan and add the lime and herbs just before serving.\n|Drizzle with a little extra olive oil if you feel it needs more dressing.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nTransfer to a large serving bowl while warm and top with crumbled [[Goats' cheese|goats' cheese]].\n\nServe with [[Home-made pitta breads|homemade pitta breads]] - they are simple to make and far superior to any shop-bought product.\n===Variations===\nTake 50% of the finished product, with or without 50% of the [[goats' cheese]], and blend in a [[food processor]], then mix back into the whole chick peas for a more interesting texture.\n===Chef's notes===\nAny of the chickpea salad unused on the day would [[freeze]] well, with or without the [[goats' cheese]] provided it is refrigerated the moment it cools.  It would keep in even better condition if it were [[vacuum packed]] first.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Algerian recipes]]\n[[Category:Lebanese recipes]]\n[[Category:Libyan recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:Moroccan recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chickpeas #chickpeasaladwithredonionsgoatscheeseandpaprika #oliveoil #lime #garlic #onions #vacuumpacked #zest #wok #boil #limezest </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Claire Sweeney's Harissa Chicken a meat recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chicken #belazu #harissapaste #houmous #harissa #honey #clairesweeneysharissachicken #avocado #salad #carrots #almonds \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A spicy chicken recipe that is served with a carrot and avocado salad, houmous and pitta bread\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1976\n|PortionCalories = 988\n|DatePublished=10th February 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 2\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 2 hours 55 minutes\n |PrepTime = 2 hours 20 minutes\n |CookTime = 35 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Claire Sweeney's Harissa Chicken recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Whoever you are Claire...</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">...this is good. Generously cover both sides with the [[Harissa]] and [[Honey|honey]] mix.\n| Use my [[Lock and Lock box]] trick to make life easier (''see pics'').\n| Leave to marinade for a few hours if you have the time.\n| Place in a [[Baking|baking]] dish on a bed of sliced [[Onions|onions]], seasoned with [[Salt|salt]], [[Pepper|pepper]] and [[Olive oil|olive oil]].\n| Cook on middle shelf for 25-35 minutes.\n| While the [[Chicken|chicken]] is cooking, mix the [[Olive oil|olive oil]], [[Balsamic vinegar|balsamic vinegar]] and [[Mustard|mustard]] in a bowl.\n| Combine the [[Carrots|carrots]] and the [[Avocado|avocado]], and stir in the dressing. Finish with some [[Almonds|almonds]].\n| Take the [[Chicken|chicken]] out of the [[Oven|oven]] and serve with the [[Salad|salad]], warm [[Flatbread|flatbread]] and a generous dollop of [[Houmous|houmous]].\n}}\n(''TV Times'')\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Chicken marinaded.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Close and shake well\nImage:Chicken and marinade.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Add the chicken and the [[harissa paste]] mixture to the Lock and lock box.\n</gallery>\n\n===Chef's notes===\nI have not yet tried the [[Belazu]] rose [[Harissa paste|harissa paste]] yet, but it cannot be a strong as my [[Harissa|harissa]] paste recipe. = 2\n |TotalTime = 18 minutes<br />Not incl overnight marinade\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 8 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Couscous tabbouleh recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Great vegetarian feast</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Especially with toasted nuts and fried chillies</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[Bulghur wheat|bulghur wheat]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 3 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 6 [[Spring onions|spring onions]], finely sliced\n| 4 [[Cloves garlic, crushed|cloves garlic, crushed]]\n| 350 ml hot [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]] (or use [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]] if your prefer)\n| 180 g [[Couscous|couscous]]\n| 3 [[Tomatoes, peeled|tomatoes, peeled]] and [[Spring onions|spring onions]] and [[Garlic|garlic]].\n| [[Fry]] until soft and golden.\n| Remove from heat, add the [[Stock|stock]] and [[Couscous|couscous]].\n| Cover and mix in the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Parsley|parsley]], [[Mint|mint]], [[Chillies|chillies]], [[Orange juice|orange juice]] and seasoning.\n| Leave to [[Marinate|marinate]] until cool or overnight.\n| Make a bed of [[Lettuce|lettuce]] on a plate or in a bowl and put the mixture on the leaves.\n| Sprinkle some [[Pine nuts|pine nuts]] over the top.\n}}\n===Variations===\nTry with [[Chopped red peppers|chopped red peppers]] and substitute fresh [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]] for the [[Parsley|parsley]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Couscous tabbouleh]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Couscous title": "Falafel",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Falafel, Garlic recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#falafel #coriander #pittabread #burghul #chickpeas #lemon #cumin #garlic #zest #jellybag #frying \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Falafel is a fried ball or patty made from spiced fava beans and/or chickpeas\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1332\n|PortionCalories = 333\n|DatePublished=31st January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 3 hours\n|PrepTime = 2 hours 45 minutes\n|CookTime = 15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Falafel.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">A wonderful mezze</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">3.8</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Great in a pitta with tzatziki</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\n'''Falafel''' is a fried ball or patty made from spiced [[fava beans]] and/or [[chickpeas]]. It is a popular form of fast food in the Arab World, where it is also served as a mezze.\n\nFalafel is usually served in [[pitta bread]], either inside the pita, which acts as a pocket, or wrapped in a flat pita. In many countries falafel is a popular street food or fast food. The falafel balls, whole or crushed, may be topped with salads, pickled vegetables and hot sauce, and drizzled with [[tahini]]-based sauces. Falafel balls may also be eaten alone as a snack or served as part of a mezze. During Ramadan, they are sometimes eaten as part of an iftar, the meal which breaks the daily fast after sunset.\n\nFalafel has been part of the diet of Egyptians and the people of the Arab World (Muslims, Christians and Mizrahi Jews among them) for centuries.\n\n==Falafel recipe==\n\nYou can buy packets of [[Falafel|falafel]] mixture but it's just as easy to make it yourself, and like all self-made meals, you can adjust the flavours to suit your tastes.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 225 g (8oz) [[Dried|dried]] [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]], soaked overnight in cold water, boiled until soft (about 2 hours) and drained\n| 75 g pitta bread, torn into pieces\n| 75 g fine [[burghul]]\n| 1 small [[onion]], peeled and chopped\n| 1 teaspoon [[Cumin|cumin]] seeds, ground\n| 1 teaspoon [[Coriander|coriander]] seeds, ground\n| 1 - 2 teaspoons [[chilli flakes]] or [[chilli powder]] (or to taste)\n| 1 - 2 [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves, peeled and crushed (or to taste)\n| 1 tablespoon fresh [[coriander]] or [[Parsley|parsley]] leaves and stalks, chopped\n| The juice and [[Zest|zest]] from &frac12; a [[Lemon|lemon]]\n| [[Sea salt]] and freshly ground [[black pepper]] to taste\n| [[Vegetable oil]] for [[Frying|frying]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Soak the pitta breads until soft\n| Soak the [[burghul]] for 15 minutes\n| Squeeze as much water out of the [[burghul]] and the [[pitta bread]], you can use a [[jelly bag]] for this\n| In a [[Coffee|coffee]] grinder or [[Mortar and pestle|mortar and pestle]], grind the [[Coriander|coriander]] and [[Cumin|cumin]] seeds.\n| Rinse and drain the [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]] and place in a [[Food processor|food processor]] with the rest of the ingredients \n| Blend until smooth\n| Shape into about 25 balls and refrigerate for 2 hours to allow the flavours to mingle.\n| Heat 5 cm (2\") of [[Oil|oil]] in a frying pan or [[Wok|wok]], or you can use a deep-fat fryer.\n| [[Deep-fry]] in batches for about 4-5 minutes, until [[Browned|browned]]. Remove with a slotted spoon and drain on kitchen paper\n}}\n===Serving suggestion===\n\nServe 3 or 4 falafel inside a warm [[pitta bread]], with a drizzle of [[Yoghurt|yogurt]] or [[garlic mayonnaise]] and a few salad leaves.\n===Variations===\nPersonally, I would add 1-2 bulbs (rather than cloves) of [[Garlic|garlic]], but leave out the [[lemon]] [[zest]].\n\nUse 1 large 400 g can of chickpeas, drained instead of dried chickpeas.\n===Chef's tip===\n\nFalafel freeze well.\n\n==See also==\n* '''[[Falafel with cucumber salad and pitta bread]]'''\n{{RecipeLine}}\n{{CategoryLineIngredients}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Lebanese recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Ingredients]]\n[[Category:Prepared foods]]\n[[Category:Deep fried]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#falafel #coriander #pittabread #burghul #chickpeas #lemon #cumin #garlic #zest #jellybag #frying </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

title": "Falafel with cucumber salad and pitta bread",
                "revisions": [

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Falafel with cucumber salad and pitta bread Vegetarian recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#falafel #coriander #cucumbersalad #bicarbonateofsoda #garlic #parsley #redonion #pittabreads #falafelwithcucumbersaladandpittabread #chickpeas #vegetableoil \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A refreshing vegetarian side salad that is a great party snack or tapa\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 5251\n|PortionCalories = 1312\n|DatePublished=20th December 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 15 minutes\n |PrepTime = 45 minutes minutes\n |CookTime = 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Falafel(2) recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Best with garlic yogurt</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Don't bother with the cucumber dressing</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\nA refreshing [[vegetarian]] side [[salad]] that is a great party snack or [[tapa]].\n\n'''For the [[Falafel]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 Medium white [[Onions|onions]], quartered\n| 3-4 Cloves [[Garlic|garlic]]\n| 2 x  410g/14&frac12; oz Cans [[Chick peas|chick peas]], drained\n| 2 Teaspoons [[Ground cumin|ground cumin]]\n| 1 Teaspoon [[Bicarbonate of soda|bicarbonate of soda]]\n| [[Salt]] and [[Cayenne pepper|cayenne pepper]]\n| 25g/1oz [[Coriander leaves]]\n| 25g/1oz [[Parsley]]\n| 4 tablespoons [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| [[Vegetable oil]] for [[Frying|frying]]\n}}\n'''For the [[Cucumber salad]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| &frac12; [[Red onion]], finely chopped\n| &frac14; [[Cucumber]], deseeded, [[Diced|diced]]\n| 2 Tablespoons fresh chopped [[Mint|mint]]\n| 150g/5oz [[Natural yogurt]]\n}}\n'''To serve'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 6 [[Pitta breads]]\n| 2 Little gem [[Lettuces|lettuces]], [[Shredded|shredded]]\n| 1 [[Red onion]], thinly sliced\n| Extra fresh [[Coriander|coriander]] to garnish\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Finely chop the [[Onion|onion]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] in a [[Food processor|food processor]]. \n| Add the [[Chick peas|chick peas]], [[Cumin|cumin]], [[Bicarbonate of soda|bicarbonate of soda]] and plenty of seasoning and blitz until a smooth paste. \n| Take out of the processor and put into a bowl.\n| Finely chop the [[Coriander|coriander]] and [[Parsley|parsley]] and stir into the [[Chickpea|chickpea]] mixture then press together into a ball.\n| Take off dessertspoons of the mixture and [[Mould|mould]] into [[Egg|egg]] shaped ovals with your hands then roll in [[Flour|flour]]. \n| Chill for 30 minutes. \n| Mix the [[Cucumber salad|cucumber salad]] ingredients together and chill.\n| Pour [[Oil|oil]] into a [[Frying pan|frying pan]] so that it is about 1 cm/&frac12; inch deep, heat up then [[Fry|fry]] the [[Falafel|falafel]] in batches, turning until crisp and golden [[Brown|brown]]. \n| Lift out of the pan with a [[Slotted spoon|slotted spoon]] and drain on kitchen paper.\n| Continue cooking the [[Falafel|falafel]] in batches until all are cooked. \n| Cook the [[Pitta breads|pitta breads]] in a hot ridged [[Frying pan|frying pan]] or under the [[Grill|grill]] until puffy. \n| Cut in half and fill with a little [[Lettuce|lettuce]], spoonfuls of the [[Cucumber salad|cucumber salad]] and [[Red onions|red onions]]. \n| Garnish with extra [[Coriander|coriander]] and serve immediately.\n}}\n==See also==\n* '''[[Falafel]]'''\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British Onions recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Lebanese recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n{{Template:British Onions attribution}}\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#falafel #coriander #cucumbersalad #bicarbonateofsoda #garlic #parsley #redonion #pittabreads #falafelwithcucumbersaladandpittabread #chickpeas #vegetableoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

grilled veg and salsa Jamie Oliver 15 minute meals recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Nom, nom, nom!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">The best when served with sour cream!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nI've been watching Jamie Oliver's 15 minute meals lately and I'm impressed with the ideas that have gone into these recipes.\n\nI'm more interested in the variations of these menus that the fact that they can be made in 15 minutes - though I doubt a mere mortal could complete them in such a short time!\n\nAnyway, this is my variation on Jamie's [[Falafel]] wraps with [[Grilled|grilled]] veg & [[Salsa|salsa]] - I've made this in 4 person quantity and we'll have this for 2 days.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n}}\n'''falafels'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 400g can of mixed [[Pulses|pulses]] or mixed [[Beans|beans]]\n| 400g can of [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]]\n| [[Zest]] of 1 [[Lemon|lemon]], finely [[Grated|grated]]\n| 1 tablespoon of [[Harissa paste|harissa paste]]\n| 1 teaspoon of [[Cumin seeds|cumin seeds]], freshly [[Ground|ground]]\n| 1 tablespoon of [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| 1 tablespoon of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] (for the [[Falafel|falafel]] mix)\n| Pinch of [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n| 1 tablespoon of  [[Olive oil|olive oil]] (to [[Fry|fry]] the falafels)\n| The stems from a bunch of [[Coriander|coriander]], chopped finely and a handful of leaves\n}}\n'''[[Tomato salsa|tomato salsa]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 3 large [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 1 fresh [[Chilli|chilli]], finely chopped\n| 1 [[Fat|fat]] [[Clove|clove]] of [[Garlic, peeled and crushed|garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| [[Juice]] and [[Grated|grated]] [[Zest|zest]] from 1 [[Lime|lime]]\n| [[Salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] to taste\n}}\n'''[[Grilled|grilled]] [[Vegetables|vegetables]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 [[Fennel bulb|fennel bulb]], thinly sliced\n| 1 medium [[Onion|onion]], thinly sliced\n| 2 [[Sweet peppers|sweet peppers]], deseeded and cut into chunks\n| 1 [[Sprig of rosemary|sprig of rosemary]]\n| 1 [[Sprig of mint|sprig of mint]]\n| [[Ground pepper]] to taste \n| [[Salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] to taste\n}}\n'''[[Side dishes|side dishes]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 pack of [[Corn tortillas|corn tortillas]]\n| 300 g tub of [[Cottage cheese|cottage cheese]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Chilli sauce]] of your choice\n| 4 tablespoons of [[Pickled red cabbage|pickled red cabbage]]\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Falafel wraps with grilled veg and salsa and cat.jpg|The spread, cat 'n all!\nImage:Jamies grilled vegetables.jpg|The grilled vegetables after 5 minutes\nImage:Jamies alternate grilled vegetables.jpg|The following day's grilled vegetable variation (''the best'')\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n'''falafels'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Drain the [[Beans|beans]] and [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]] and dry them really well.  A [[Salad spinner|salad spinner]] is a good way to do this.  They need to be really dry or the falafels will not stick together.  \n| Tip them into the [[Food processor|food processor]] with all the [[Falafel|falafel]] ingredients and [[Blend|blend]] to a fairly fine paste\n| Using wetted hands, form the [[Falafel|falafel]] mix into about 12 balls and press them flat so there is a good surface to [[Fry|fry]] and [[Brown|brown]]\n| [[Fry]] then is a tablespoon of [[Olive oil|olive oil]], turn them once they have [[Browned|browned]] , the less you handle them, the less chance these is of them falling apart. Don't worry if they fall apart - mine did!  They are going in a [[Tortilla|tortilla]] wrap anyway.\n}}\n'''[[Grilled|grilled]] [[Vegetables|vegetables]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add a spay of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] to your [[Griddle pan|griddle pan]] and throw in all of the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] for [[Grilling|grilling]] together with the [[Herbs|herbs]]\n| Gill for 10 minutes or more, turning now and then\n| Add the [[Juice|juice]] of half a [[Lemon|lemon]] just before you serve\n}}\n'''[[Salsa|salsa]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], chopped [[Chilli|chilli]], [[Coriander|coriander]] stems and leaves, [[Crushed garlic|crushed garlic]], [[Lime juice|lime juice]] and [[Zest|zest]] and seasoning to the [[Food processor|food processor]] and blitz until it  gets to your desired consistency - chill if you have the time\n}}\n'''[[Cottage cheese|cottage cheese]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Stir in a tablespoon of [[Chilli sauce|chilli sauce]] to add some colour and bite\n}}\n'''[[Corn tortillas|corn tortillas]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Microwave]] for 45 seconds just to moisten them and warm them a little\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nSpread everything out and tuck in!\n===Recipe source===\n\n* Idea from Jamie Oliver's 15 minute meals TV series\n===Variations===\nTry you own variation on [[Herbs|herbs]] and [[Spices|spices]]\n\n[[Courgettes]] and [[Carrots|carrots]] make a nice change for the [[Grilled|grilled]] vegetables.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Lebanese recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#falafel #grilled #oliveoil #fry #vegetables #zest #herbs #beans #chillisauce #cottagecheese #salsa </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
