title": "Falafel wraps with Taste Sensation dips",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Falafel wraps with Taste Sensation dips\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#tastesensation #meatballs #rocket #dips #oliveoil #tomatoes #vegetarian #lemonjuice #tortilla #greekyogurt #yogurt \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=IKEAs Meat Free vegetarian meatballs in wraps with rocket and dips\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|DatePublished=22nd February 2020\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  1 hour, 25 minutes\n|PrepTime =  1 hour, 10 minutes\n|CookTime =  15 minutes\n|TotalCalories = 1770\n|PortionCalories = 885 \n|Image = [[Image:Falafel wraps with Taste Sensation dips recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Taste Sensation-tastic!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Just love their spices.  I could eat them straight of of the bag - and often do.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nI accidentally bought IKEA's '[[Meat]] Free' vegetarian [[Meatballs|meatballs]]. I would now buy them in preference to the actual meatballs.  They are lovely; a sort of herby [[Falafel|falafel]].  Having worked that one out, I thought this would be a good opportunity to try some of my new [[Taste Sensation|Taste Sensation]] powders as they make great [[Dips|dips]] when added to [[Yogurt|yogurt]].  The [[Rocket|rocket]] just completes these wraps.  They were fab!\n\nWhen I've made the [[Yogurt|yogurt]] [[Dips|dips]] with [[Taste Sensation]] powders, I've found they mix in better if left for a while, though if you're pushed for time, just make sure you mix them well instead.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 20 Ikea [[Vegetarian]] '[[Meat]]-Free' [[Meatballs|meatballs]], ''read '[[Falafel]]'''\n| 6 white [[Tortilla|tortilla]] wraps\n| 70 g bag of [[Rocket|rocket]]\n| 6 [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| Splash of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| Splash of [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]]\n}}\n====for four dips====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 400 g [[Greek yogurt|Greek yogurt]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Taste Sensation Tomato powder]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Taste Sensation]] [[Lime juice|lime juice]] powder\n| 1 teaspoon [[Taste Sensation]] Sweet [[Chilli]] [[Marinade]] flavouring\n| 1 teaspoon [[Taste Sensation Piri Piri seasoning]]\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:FalafelsreadyToWrap.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Falafel / veggie meatballs; ready to wrap\nImage:TasteSensation yogurt dips.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Assorted [[Taste Sensation yogurt dips]]\n</gallery>\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Mix up the [[Dips|dips]] and leave for 1 hour, then stir again before use.\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n}}\n====the dips====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| For each of the [[Dips|dips]], add a teaspoon of the flavouring powders to three tablespoons of [[Greek yogurt]] and mix well.  Leave to stand for one hour if you have the time.\n}}\n====the wraps====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add IKEA's [[Meat|meat]]-free [[Meatballs|meatballs]] to a [[Lock and Lock box]], add a splash of [[Olive oil|olive oil]], pop the lid on and shake well.  I find this gives them a nice crispy coat.\n| Pop them in the [[Air Fryer]] for 15 minutes\n| [[Microwave]] the [[Tortilla|tortilla]] wraps for 20 seconds to warm them slightly\n| Tip the [[Rocket|rocket]] into a bowl and make a simple [[Salad dressing|salad dressing]] with 1 tablespoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and a shake of [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]]\n| Chop the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nSmear the [[Tortillas|tortillas]] with a [[Dip|dip]] or [[Dips of your choice|dips of your choice]], add [[Rocket|rocket]], [[falafels]] and [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], roll them up and eat them - carefully!\n===Chef's notes===\nIf you don't have an [[Air-fryer]] you can [[Oven|oven]] [[Bake|bake]] the [[Vegetarian|vegetarian]] [[Meatballs|meatballs]] for 15 minutes at 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4), fan oven 160\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour or pan fry in a little [[Olive oil|olive oil]] for 10 minutes,.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Lebanese recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:Swedish recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Air fried recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n[[Category:Taste Sensation recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#tastesensation #meatballs #rocket #dips #oliveoil #tomatoes #vegetarian #lemonjuice #tortilla #greekyogurt #yogurt </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Fatayer",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Fatayer a cheese recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#fatayer #dough #flour #hand #oliveoil #garlic #cheese #breadmaker #squash #wintersquash #yeast \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Fatayer is a pastry that can be stuffed with spinach (sabaneq), cheese (jibnah) or meat\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1165\n|PortionCalories = 291\n|DatePublished=22nd October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 3\n |TotalTime = 2 hours 30 minutes\n |PrepTime = 2 hours\n |CookTime = 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Fatayer recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Lebanese 'Cornish' pasties</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.2</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Although they could not be sold as such! \ud83d\ude01</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\nFatayer is a pastry that can be stuffed with [[Spinach|spinach]] (sabaneq), [[Cheese|cheese]] (jibnah) or [[Meat|meat]]. It is part of [[Middle Eastern cuisine]] and is eaten in [[Turkey]], Syria, Lebanon, Jordan and other countries in the region.\n\nThis version using [[Winter squash|winter squash]] is based on a recipe in Sam & Sam Clarkes' excellent '[[Moro]]' cookbook - ISBN 9780091880842\n\n\n'''For the  Fatayer [[Dough|dough]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 220 g [[Strong white bread flour|strong white bread flour]]\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Dried active yeast|dried active yeast]]\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| &#189; teaspoon fine [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 100 ml (100g) tepid water\n| 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n}}\n'''For the Fatayer filling'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 800g [[Orange|orange]] fleshed sweet [[Winter squash|winter squash]] such as Hubbard, Festival, Butternut. Peeled and de-seeded and cut into 5 cm (2\") chunks\n| 1 tablespoon [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 1 Clove of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| 100g [[Feta cheese|feta cheese]], crumbled with 1 tablespoon freshly chopped [[Marjoram|marjoram]] or [[Oregano|oregano]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Toasted|toasted]] pinenuts\n| &#188; teaspoon [[Ground cumin|ground cumin]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 230\u00b0 C (450\u00b0 F - gas 8), [fan oven 210\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n===Method===\n\n\n'''Making the fatayer [[Dough|dough]] with a [[Breadmaker|breadmaker]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add all of the [[Dough|dough]] ingredients to your [[Breadmaker|breadmaker]]\n| Set to ''[[Dough|dough]]'' or ''[[Pizza|pizza]]'' setting\n| Wait for an hour , remove the perfect [[Dough|dough]]. If the dough s to wet add a little more [[Flour|flour]] and repeat the cycle, more water if too dry.\n}}\n'''Making the fatayer [[Dough|dough]] by [[Hand|hand]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Sift the [[Flour|flour]] into a bowl\n| Warm the water to body temperature.\n| Take a few tablespoons of the warm water, add the [[Sugar|sugar]] and [[Yeast|yeast]] and leave in a warm place for 15 minutes.\n| Stir the [[Salt|salt]] and [[Oil|oil]] into the remaining water.\n| Add the [[Yeast|yeast]] mixture to the [[Flour|flour]]  and little by little, add the remaining water, massaging the lumps out by [[Hand|hand]].\n| Once you have added all of the water and you have a manageable lump, transfer to a [[Flour|flour]]ed surface and [[Kneading bread|knead]] by [[Hand|hand]] for about 10 minutes or until soft and elastic but not tacky.  Add more [[Flour|flour]] or water to get to the correct consistency.\n| Cover with a damp [[Tea-towel|tea-towel]] and leave in a warm place of about an hour.\n'''Preparing the [[Butternut squash|butternut squash]] filling'''\n| Toss the cubed sqush in a bowl with the [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and a grind of [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| [[Roast]] on a [[Baking tray|baking tray]] for about 20 minutes or until you can squish the [[Squash|squash]] with your finger.\n| Allow to cool a little and then [[Mash|mash]] to a pur\u00e9e. Season to taste.\n}}\n'''Making the fatayers'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Divide the [[Dough|dough]] into 4 balls.  Roll each ball into an 18cm (7\") disc.\n| Divide the remaining ingredients into four and place in the centre of each disc, [[Squash|squash]] first, [[Cheese|cheese]] last.\n| [[Brush]] the edges of the discs with a little water so they stick better and then shape to a small pyramid and squeeze the joins together to seal.\n| Trim and discard any excess [[Dough|dough]].\n| [[Bake]] for 15 minutes until lightly coloured, but not crisp.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a [[Green salad|green salad]] and [[Tahini|tahini]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Lebanese recipes]]\n[[Category:Libyan recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#fatayer #dough #flour #hand #oliveoil #garlic #cheese #breadmaker #squash #wintersquash #yeast </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]

title": "Fattoush",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Fattoush, Vegetarian recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#fattoush #vegetables #sumac #diced #herbs #pittabread #fried #lemonjuice #cabbage #parsley #springonions \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Fattoush, pronounced \"fadash\", is a Levantine salad made from several garden vegetables and toasted or fried pieces of pita bread\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1107\n|PortionCalories = 276\n|DatePublished=24th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 15 minutes\n|PrepTime = 15 minutes\n|CookTime = None\n|Image = [[Image:Fattoush recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Delicious veggie meal</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Thanks Julia - this was superb!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\nFattoush, pronounced \"fadash\", is a Levantine [[salad]] made from several garden [[vegetables]] and [[toasted]] or [[fried]] pieces of [[pita bread]]. Fattoush salad allows cooks to use seasonal produce by mixing different [[vegetables]] and [[herbs]] according to taste, and also to make use of pitas that have gone stale. The vegetables are cut into relatively larges pieces compared to [[Tabbouleh]] which requires ingredients to be finely chopped. [[Sumac]] is usually used to give Fattoush its sour taste.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 [[cucumber]], peeled, deseeded and [[diced]]\n| 6 tablespoons [[extra virgin olive oil]]\n| 3 [[pitta breads]], split in two and cut into 2.5 cm (1\") squares\n| 2 tablespoons torn fresh [[coriander leaves]]\n| 2 tablespoons roughly chopped fresh [[mint]]\n| 2 tablespoons roughly chopped fresh [[parsley]]\n| 1 [[red onion]], cut into 1cm/&frac12;in dice\n| 5 ripe [[Tomatoes, roasted and peeled|tomatoes, peeled, deseeded]] and cut into 1cm/&frac12;in dice\n| 2 [[green bell peppers]], deseeded and cut into thin strips\n| 2 [[cloves of garlic, crushed]]\n| 1 tablespoon of [[sumac]] or the juice of 1 [[lemon]]\n| [[Salt]] and [[freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat 2 tablespoons of the [[oil]] in a [[frying]] pan and [[fry]] the [[pitta bread]] until it is golden brown. Drain on kitchen paper to remove any excess oil\n| Alternatively, cook the [[pitta bread]] using our [[crisp bread]] recipe, then cut into squares\n| Add the [[Garlic|garlic]], [[lemon juice]], remaining [[olive oil]] and the [[herbs]] into a bowl and mix well to make the dressing\n| Put the [[diced]] [[vegetables]] in a large bowl and pour the dressing over the [[vegetables]] and toss well\n| Season to taste with [[salt]] and [[pepper]], garnish with the strips of [[fried]] [[bread]]\n}}\n===Variations===\n\nThere are many variations for this recipe, some alternative ingredients might be:\n*[[Lettuce]]\n*[[Spring onions]]\n*[[Feta cheese]]\n*[[Carrots]]\n*[[Red peppers]]\n*[[Green peppers]]\n*[[Cabbage]]\n*[[Black olives]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#fattoush #vegetables #sumac #diced #herbs #pittabread #fried #lemonjuice #cabbage #parsley #springonions </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

It's absolutely gorgeous on its own but goes well on the side of all sorts of [[Pork|pork]] and [[Fish dishes|fish dishes]]\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 200g [[Freekeh]] \n| 2 [[Fennel|fennel]] bulbs, trimmed and thinly sliced. If there are any fronds at the top, reserve for garnish \n| 2 [[Leeks|leeks]], washed and thinly sliced \n| 2 [[Courgettes|courgettes]], thinly sliced or spiralised \n| 1 tablespoon [[Coriander seeds|coriander seeds]], lightly crushed \n| A small handful each of fresh [[Mint leaves|mint leaves]], [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]] and curly [[Parsley|parsley]], finely chopped \n| 150g [[Green olives|green olives]], quartered \n| 100g [[Blanched|blanched]] [[Almonds|almonds]], [[Toasted|toasted]] and roughly chopped \n| 1 small hot [[Chilli|chilli]], very finely chopped \n| [[Juice]] of half a [[Lemon|lemon]] \n| 1 tablespoon [[White wine|white wine]] or [[Rice vinegar|rice vinegar]] \n| [[Extra virgin Olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]] \n| [[Salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat your [[Oven|oven]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4), [fan oven 160\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Turn the [[Oven|oven]] on to 180C/gas mark 4. Set the freekeh soaking in cold water. \n| Put the [[Fennel|fennel]], [[Leeks|leeks]] and [[Courgettes|courgettes]] on a backing tray in one layer. Season with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]], give them a good drizzle of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and sprinkle with the crushed [[Coriander seeds|coriander seeds]]. Put them in the [[Oven|oven]] when it\u0092s up to temperature, setting your timer for 20 minutes \n| When the freekeh has been soaking for 20 minutes, drain and put into a [[Saucepan|saucepan]] with 750mls of water. Put on a medium heat and bring gently to a [[Boil|boil]]. Lower the heat and [[Simmer|simmer]] for about 12 minutes, or just tender and chewy. Drain and set aside \n| When the veggies have been [[Baking|baking]] for 20 minutes, check them for texture and flavour. They should be cooked, but still have a good bite to them, with the [[Leeks|leeks]] in particular nice and crispy around the edges. As soon as they\u0092re done, sprinkle with a little of the [[Vinegar|vinegar]] and set aside. When they\u0092're cool, gently mix the chopped [[Herbs|herbs]] in. Set aside \n| In a bowl, put the [[Olives|olives]], [[Almonds|almonds]], [[Chilli|chilli]] and [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]]. Stir well, and set aside \n| When you\u0092re ready to serve, combine the freekeh, the [[Veggie|veggie]] mix and the [[Olive|olive]] mix. Taste, adjust the seasoning with [[Salt|salt]], [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]], if you need to, garnish with the [[Fennel|fennel]] fronds, and serve\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Nik and Edwina's Cookbook recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#fennel #leeks #chilli #courgettes #corianderseeds #oliveoil #almonds #lemonjuice #fennelolivefreekehandherbsalad #baking #pork </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Any excuse to use my pomegranate molasses\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2383\n|PortionCalories = 595\n|DatePublished=23rd October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4 as a [[Starter|starter]]\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 35 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 20 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Fried kidneys in pomegranate molasses recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n======Best recipe review======\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Highly unusual!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">And very nice, though the pomegranate molasses can be quite hard to find.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis is my take on a recipe found in a [translated] Lebanese cook-book from around 1960.  Any excuse to use my [[Pomegranate molasses|pomegranate molasses]].  The original recipe specifies lambs [[Kidneys|kidneys]], I would reduce the number to 4 if you are using [[Beef|beef]] kidneys.\n\nI have kept the original quantities, however for the [[Sake|sake]] of your health, I would reduce the amount of [[salt]] and [[butter]] (or use 50/50 with [[olive oil]]).\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 8 Lambs [[Kidneys|kidneys]]\n| 6 oz [[Butter|butter]] [see note above]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Salt|salt]] [see note above]\n| 4 oz sour [[Pomegranate|pomegranate]] [[Juice|juice]] - Made up from about 1 part [[Pomegranate molasses|pomegranate molasses]] to 3 parts water and mixed well\n| 1 oz [[Garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Spice]] mix [below]\n| Few tablespoons [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| Chopped [[Parsley|parsley]] to garnish\n}}\n'''[[Spice|spice]] mix'''\n* Equal quantities, [[Cinnamon|cinnamon]], [[White cumin|white cumin]], [[Chilli powder|chilli powder]] and [[Paprika|paprika]], mixed together and finely [[Ground|ground]].\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Cut the [[Kidneys|kidneys]] in half lengthwise, trim and remove the skins.\n| Flatten them under a cleaver or a heavy pan, [cut into small pieces if desired]\n| Heat the [[Butter|butter]] and [[Fry|fry]] the [[Kidneys|kidneys]] on both sides until [[Browned|browned]].\n| Remove the [[Kidneys|kidneys]] and keep warm.\n| Fry the garlic until it starts to colour.\n| Add the [[Spice|spice]] mixture and [[Salt|salt]] to the [[Flour|flour]] and mix into what remains of the [[Butter|butter]].\n| Stir until it just begins to [[Brown|brown]] then add the [[Pomegranate|pomegranate]] [[Juice|juice]], allow to [[Boil|boil]], return the [[Kidneys|kidneys]] and cook for a few minutes in the [[Sauce|sauce]].\n| Serve hot garnished with [[parsley]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nThe original recipe suggests [[Fried|fried]] or pur\u00e9ed [[Potatoes|potatoes]].  I think it would go nicely with [[Brown|brown]] toast as a [[Starter|starter]].\n===Chef's note===\nWell this was an interesting dish.  I think when I make it again I will brown the kidneys first over a very high heat, in a little oil, and then continue with the sauce.  It was fine with half the butter and mush less salt.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Kidneys]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes|Kidneys]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes|Kidneys]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes|Kidneys]]\n[[Category:Lamb recipes|Kidneys]]\n[[Category:Lebanese recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes|Kidneys]]\n[[Category:North African recipes|Kidneys]]\n[[Category:Starters|Kidneys]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#kidneys #butter #spice #friedkidneysinpomegranatemolasses #pomegranate #parsley #pomegranatemolasses #starter #juice #boil #unusualrecipes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Ful medames",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Ful medames, Garlic recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#fulmedames #beans #oliveoil #onion #salad #favabeans #bread #garlic #fulbeans #cumin #pittabreads \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Ful medames also Foul Mudammas is one of the national dishes of Sudan and Egypt, often eaten at breakfast\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2703\n|PortionCalories = 675\n|DatePublished=19th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 16 hours, 10 minutes\n |PrepTime = 12 hours 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 4 hours\n |Image = [[Image:Ful medames recipe.jpg|220px|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Looks nasty, tastes ok</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">3.4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">They say you eat with your eyes.  'Nuff said. </span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n'''Ful medames''' also '''Foul Mudammas'''  is one of the national dishes of Sudan and Egypt, often eaten at breakfast. It consists of brown [[Fava beans|fava beans]], partially or completely [[Mashed|mashed]], which are slow-cooked and served with [[Olive oil|olive oil]], chopped [[Parsley|parsley]], [[Onion|onion]], [[Garlic|garlic]], and [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]]. Ful medames is typically eaten with Egyptian [[Bread|bread]] ('eish masri).\n\nThe dish's name derives from the Egyptian language: ful is the Egyptian word for [[Fava beans|fava beans]], and medames is a Coptic word meaning \"buried.\" The second word hints at the original cooking method, which involved burying a sealed pot of water and [[Beans|beans]] under hot coals. This cooking method for [[Beans|beans]] is mentioned in the Jerusalem Talmud, indicating that it has been used in the Middle East at least since the 4th century.\n\nFul medames was exported from Egypt to the Arab World, particularly the Levant and Somalia. Ful medames came to the Horn of Africa when the Egyptians captured Zeila in the beginning of the 19th century. From there, it spread to other regions. In northern Somalia, ful is eaten with a [[Pancake|pancake]]-like [[Bread|bread]] called [[laxoox]]. Ful is also part of Ethiopian cuisine, where it is served with [[flatbread]] and [[mitmita powder]] or [[berebere spice mix]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 450 g (1 lb) [[ful beans]], soaked overnight, rinsed and drained\n| 1 tablespoon\tfreshly [[Ground cumin|ground cumin]]\n| 6 [[Cloves garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| 4 [[Hard-boiled eggs|hard-boiled eggs]], shelled and coarsely chopped\n| 1 handful [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]], chopped\n| 1 handful fresh [[Mint leaves|mint leaves]], chopped \n| 2 [[Lemons|lemons]], cut into quarters\n| 1 [[Spanish]] [[Onion|onion]], peeled and sliced\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n'''To serve'''\n* [[Olive oil]]\n* 6 [[Pitta breads]]\n* 200 ml [[Yogurt]]\n* 4 [[Tomatoes]]\n* Half a [[Cucumber|cucumber]]\n* 150 g Mixed [[Salad|salad leaves]]\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[oven]] to 120\u00b0 C (250\u00b0 F - gas &frac12;), [fan oven 100\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Place the presoaked [[Beans|beans]] in a [[Casserole dish|casserole dish]], fill with water and cover the [[Beans|beans]] by 2 inches    \n| Add half of the [[Cumin|cumin]], Crushed [[Garlic|garlic]] and lots of [[Black pepper|black pepper]], cover and cook for 4 hours until the [[Beans|beans]] are soft.  Don't break the [[Beans|beans]] up.\n| Place the [[Eggs|eggs]], [[Herbs|herbs]], [[Onion|onion]] slices and [[Lemon|lemon]] quarters on separate plates\n| When the [[Beans|beans]] are cooked, stir in the remaining [[Cumin|cumin]] and add [[Salt|salt]] to taste\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe the [[Baking|baking]] dish at the table with the plates of garnish, [[Olive oil|olive oil]], [[Pitta breads|pitta breads]] and [[Salad|salad]]\n===Variations===\nIf you cannot get [[ful beans]], other [[Dried beans|dried beans]] will suffice, though the flavour will not be the same\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Breakfast recipes]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#fulmedames #beans #oliveoil #onion #salad #favabeans #bread #garlic #fulbeans #cumin #pittabreads </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

title": "Harra bi isbaou",
                "revisions": [
                    {

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Harra bi isbaou, Vegetarian recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#lentils #dough #oliveoil #onions #harrabiisbaou #coriander #tamarind #pasta #lemonjuice #fry #restfor \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Harra Bi IsbaA\u0092ou literary means (burn in his finger), is an old Syrian-Damascene\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 4225\n|PortionCalories = 704\n|DatePublished=18th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = 6\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  1 hour, 10 minutes\n|PrepTime =  25 minutes\n|CookTime =  45 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Harra bi isbaou recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n}}\n\nHarra Bi Isba\u00c2\u0092ou (&#1581;&#1585;&#1575;&#1569; &#1576;&#1575;&#1589;&#1576;&#1593;&#1608;) literary means (burn in his finger), is an old Syrian- Damascene [[Vegetarian dish|vegetarian dish]]. Based on [[Lentils|lentils]] and [[Bread|bread]] [[Dough|dough]] and usually served with pickled [[Cucumber|cucumber]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients \n| 3 cups of [[Plain flour|plain flour]]\n| 1 1/4cup water\n| 1/2tsp.  [[Salt|salt]]\n}}\n\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB \n| 2 cup [[Brown|brown]] [[Lentils|lentils]]\n| 2 tsp. [[Salt|salt]]\n| &#189; cup of soaked [[Tamarind]] or you can use &frac14; cup of [[Pomegranate molasses|pomegranate molasses]] instead.\n| 3 tablespoons [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] and more if needed\n| 1/4 cup [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 6 medium [[Onions|onions]] thinly sliced\n| 3 bunches of fresh [[Coriander|coriander]] (chopped)\n| 6[[Cloves|cloves]] of [[Crushed garlic|crushed garlic]]\n| 1 [[Pomegranate|pomegranate]], deseeded\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Starting with the [[Dough|dough]]. In a bowl mix the [[Flour|flour]] with water and [[Salt|salt]]. \n| [[Knead]] the [[Dough|dough]] from 3-4 minutes till you get a smooth and stretchy [[Dough|dough]]. Cover and let it [[Rest for|rest for]] 20 minutes.\n| On a floured surface, roll out the [[Dough|dough]] for about &frac14; cm thin and cut into long stripes then in to squares.\n| To cook the [[Lentils|lentils]], place them  in a pan and cover with water and some [[Salt|salt]] on medium heat  for 20-30 minutes or till they are cooked.\n| Add the [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] and [[Tamarind|tamarind]] or the [[Pomegranate molasses|pomegranate molasses]] to the [[Lentils|lentils]].\n| Add the [[Dough|dough]] you prepared into squares gradually in to the [[Lentils|lentils]] and keep stirring to prevent them from sticking together. Leave some for garnish. If you are using [[Pasta|pasta]] instead add it now and stir it into the [[Lentils|lentils]], cover it till it is cooked.\n| [[Deep fry]] the [[Dough|dough]] squares you saved for garnish till they are gold and [[Brown|brown]]. Or if you used [[Pasta|pasta]] earlier on, [[Fry|fry]] some [[Flat bread|flat bread]] instead of the [[Dough|dough]].\n| In the same [[Oil|oil]] [[Fry|fry]] the [[Onions|onions]], add half of them to the [[Lentils|lentils]] and save the [[Rest for|rest for]] garnishing.\n| Add half the quantity of the [[Crushed garlic|crushed garlic]] to the [[Lentils|lentils]].\n| In a [[Frying pan|frying pan]] saut\u00e9 the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Coriander|coriander]] lightly with some [[Olive oil|olive oil]].\n| In serving dish put the [[Lentils|lentils]] you cooked earlier, heat quarter a cup of [[Olive oil|olive oil]] and pour it into the [[Lentils|lentils]].\n| Garnish with the [[Onions|onions]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Coriander|coriander]], [[Fried|fried]] [[Bread|bread]] or [[Dough|dough]] and [[Pomegranate seeds|pomegranate seeds]].\n| You can serve hot or cold.\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n\n* [http://www.manalonline.com/recipes/%D8%AD%D8%B1%D8%A7%D9%82-%D8%A7%D8%B5%D8%A8%D8%B9%D9%88 www.manalonline.com]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Strange food</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">3</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">This does not appeal.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Ethnic ]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Ethnic ]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Ethnic ]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered|Ethnic ]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:Syrian recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#lentils #dough #oliveoil #onions #harrabiisbaou #coriander #tamarind #pasta #lemonjuice #fry #restfor </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Makes about 750 mls\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 1 day, 1 hour, 10 minutes (including soaking time)\n|PrepTime = 1 day, 10 minutes (including soaking time)\n|CookTime =  1 hour\n|Image = [[Image:Hummus 2 TM recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Bicarbonate to treat chickpeas</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">A neat idea, and it worked!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Sue_spins|Susie]] </span></span>\n}}\nA recipe using [[Dried|dried]] [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]] rather than tinned or jarred and making a soft textured [[Hummus|hummus]]\n{{RecipeIngredientsTM\n| 200g [[Dried|dried]] [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Bicarbonate of soda|bicarbonate of soda]]\n| 1.2kg tap water\n| A further \u00bd teaspoon [[Bicarbonate of soda|bicarbonate of soda]]\n| 6 tablespoons [[Tahini|tahini]]\n| 6 [[Cloves|cloves]] [[Garlic|garlic]] (or to taste), crushed to a paste\n| The [[Juice|juice]] of 1 large [[Lemon|lemon]]\n| 100g water from the [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]]\n| 40-50g [[Extra virgin Olive oil|extra virgin olive oil]]\n| [[Coriander leaves]], to taste\n| [[Salt]]\n| Extra EVOO\n| [[Smoked paprika]], eg Piment\u00f3n de La Vera\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Place the [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]] and [[Bicarbonate of soda|bicarbonate of soda]] in a jug and cover with twice the volume of water.  Leave to soak for 12-24 hours.\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Drain the soaking water from the [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]], rinse and drain again.\n| Place the [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]] in the internal [[Steaming|steaming]] basket and the tap water and \u00bd teaspoons [[Bicarbonate of soda|bicarbonate of soda]] in the bowl '''50 minutes / 100\u00b0C / Speed 1'''.\n| The skins should be loosening and the [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]] soft - if not, cook for a further 10 minutes.\n| Drain (reserving some of the liquid) and leave the [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]] to cool.\n| Remove the skins if a very smooth [[Hummus|hummus]] is desired.\n| To the bowl (no need to wash) mix the [[Tahini|tahini]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] with a handful of the [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]] '''30 seconds / Speeds 5-7-9'''.\n| Scrape down the inside of the bowl.\n| Add the remaining [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]], the [[Chickpea|chickpea]] water and the [[Oil|oil]] '''30 seconds / Speeds 5-7-9'''.\n| Add the [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]] '''30 seconds / Speeds 6-8-10''' or until you have the desired fineness of [[Coriander|coriander]].\n| Serve in dishes drizzled with the extra [[Oil|oil]] and sprinkled with the [[Paprika|paprika]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with pieces of [[Vegetables|vegetables]] and [[Flat breads|flat breads]] suitable cut for dunking\n===Variations===\nIf you want a more textured [[Hummus|hummus]], reduce the blending times and speeds accordingly.\n\nTinned or jarred [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]] can be used (about 275g) but because they haven't been soaked or cooked with [[Bicarbonate of soda|bicarbonate of soda]], a very smooth result will be more difficult to achieve.\n==See also==\n\n* [[Houmous variations]]\n* title": "Hummus recipe",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Hummus recipe Greek, from Cookipedia.Co.Uk\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#chickpeas #hummusrecipe #dried #garlic #oliveoil #zest #tahini #miseenplace #freeze #lemon #dip \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This delicious dip is simple to make and extremely economical if made with dried chickpeas. The recipe given is for 125 g (4 oz) of chickpeas, though\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}} \n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 647\n|PortionCalories = 161\n|DatePublished=17th January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Hummus, served!\n |Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 2 days, 1 hour, 15 minutes\n |PrepTime = 2 days, 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour\n |Image = [[Image:How to cook hummus.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">So Easy!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">This could not be more simple - and it tastes fantastic, especially withj chips!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis delicious [[Dip|dip]] is simple to make and extremely economical if made with [[Dried|dried]] [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]].\n\nThe recipe given is for 125 g (4 oz) of [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]], though if you are making it, it's probably better to multiply the quantities and make more then [[Freeze|freeze]] the excess as it freezes really well.\nThe amount of [[Garlic|garlic]] that you add is personal taste. I use much more normally.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 125 g (4 oz) [[Dried|dried]] [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]] or 1 large can of chickpeas [about 400g of cooked chickpeas] and omit the soaking stage.\n| [[Zest]] and [[Juice|juice]] of 1 [[Lemon|lemon]]\n| 2 tablespoons light [[Tahini|tahini]]\n| 2 Cloves [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled\n| 120 ml (4 fl oz) [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] to taste\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Soak the [[Dried|dried]] [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]] for 24 hours in cold water, refreshing a few times if you can.\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n| ''If using canned [[chick peas]], just drain and rinse them with fresh water a few times and go directly to Adding them to the food processor step.''\n| Drain and rinse the soaked [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]].\n| Add to a large pan, cover with water. '''Do not add any [[Salt|salt]]''', otherwise the peas will not absorb the water properly. Bring to the [[Boil|boil]] and [[Simmer|simmer]] for 1 hour or until softened.  They may take a little longer depending on size and age. A pinch of [[baking soda]] (bicarbonate of soda) added to the cooking water will shorten the cooking time.\n| Drain, rinse and allow to cool.\n| Add to a [[Food processor|food processor]] with everything but the [[Olive oil|olive oil]]. Blend to a paste, then as if making [[Mayonnaise|mayonnaise]], gradually drizzle in the [[Olive|olive]] [[Oil|oil]] with the motor running.\n| Taste and adjust the seasoning if needed.  You can always add extra [[Garlic|garlic]] if needed.\n| Adjust the consistency by adding more oil if too thick or a handful of breadcrumbs if it is too liquid.\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Hummus recipe blending.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Blending the hummus\nImage:Chickpeas cooked.jpg|thumb|300px|right|500g of cooked chickpeas\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Crispbread|crispbread]] or [[Pittas|pittas]].\n===Variations===\nOmit the [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]], [[Zest|zest]] and [[Salt|salt]]. Instead, add the rind of a quarter of a [[Preserved lemon|preserved lemon]] plus 2 tablespoons of the [[Preserved lemon juice|preserved lemon juice]]. [[Preserved lemon hummus|Bulk recipe here!]]. \n\nYou can also cook the chickpeas in a pressure cooker - [[Chickpeas#How_to_cook_chickpeas_in_a_pressure_cooker|details here]]\n===Variations===\nAny tinned beans or pulses work well in this recipe.  I've just made a lovely batch using a mixture of [[cannellini beans]] & [[chick peas]].\n{{SeeAlsoHummus}}\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Hummus]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Hummus]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces|Hummus]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes|Hummus]]\n[[Category:Greek recipes|Hummus]]\n[[Category:Lebanese recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes|Hummus]]\n[[Category:North African recipes|Hummus]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Hummus]]\n[[Category:Starters|Hummus]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Turkish recipes|Hummus]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Hummus]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#chickpeas #hummusrecipe #dried #garlic #oliveoil #zest #tahini #miseenplace #freeze #lemon #dip </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

East and surrounding countries.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| '''''For the shells:'''''\n| 250 g (8 oz) [[burghul]] (cracked wheat) \n| 500 g (1 lb) minced [[beef]] \n| 1 [[onion]], roughly chopped \n| '''''Assembly:'''''\n| Take an egg-sized portion of the shell mixture and roll into a ball\n| Poke a hole in it with your finger and enlarge the hole to make a tiny container\n| Press some stuffing into the hole and pinch the top to make a seal. They should be 'pointy' at each end. \"[[kibbeh|Lebanese torpedoes]]\n| [[Deep fry]] in small batches until golden brown\n| Drain on kitchen towel and serve hot.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nServe with wedges of [[lemon]] or [[lime]], and though probably not authentic, [[sour cream and chive dip]] goes really well with this dish.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Lebanese recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Deep fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#onion #kibbeh #beef #burghul #kibbehrecipe #deepfry #fry #whitecumin #deepfrying #foodprocessor #browned </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                "revisions": [

                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Kidreh (Mutton with rice), Garlic recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#rice #mutton #butter #saffron #onion #stock #garlic #casseroledish #groundallspice #groundcinnamon #bayleaves \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This traditional rice recipe is from Palestine\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 4382\n|PortionCalories = 1095\n|DatePublished=20th December 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4 to 6\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 2 hours 15 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 2 hours\n |Image = [[Image:Kidreh (Mutton with rice) recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Buttery mutton</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.23</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">\ud83d\ude0b\ud83d\ude0b\ud83d\ude0b</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis traditional rice recipe is from Palestine.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 kg [[Shoulder|shoulder]] or leg of [[Mutton|mutton]], cut into chunks\n| 2 [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Salt|salt]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Ground black pepper|ground black pepper]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Ground allspice|ground allspice]]\n| &frac14; teaspoon [[Nutmeg|nutmeg]]\n| &frac14; teaspoon [[Ground|ground]] [[Cardamom|cardamom]]\n| A pinch of [[Ground cinnamon|ground cinnamon]]\n| 1 [[Onion|onion]], peeled and left whole\n| 600 g round [[Rice|rice]] - I used arborio as it soaks up juices well.\n| Pinch of [[Saffron|saffron]], pounded\n| 4 bulbs [[Garlic]], (or to taste), crushed\n| 50 g samneh ([[Clarified butter|clarified butter]]) or [[Butter|butter]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Place the [[Mutton|mutton]], [[Spices|spices]] and the whole [[Onion|onion]] in a pan and cover with water.\n| Simmer gently for 1&frac14; hours or more until the [[Meat|meat]] is tender.\n| Lightly grease a large [[Casserole dish|casserole dish]] and add the [[Rice|rice]] to it.\n| Strain the [[Mutton|mutton]] into a [[Colander|colander]] but keep the [[Stock|stock]].\n| Measure the [[Stock|stock]] and add enough hot water to bring it up to 1.1 [[Litres|litres]].\n| Pour over the [[Rice|rice]] and add the [[Saffron|saffron]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and samneh or [[Butter|butter]].\n| Place the cooked [[Meat|meat]] on the top, cover and cook for 30 minutes at 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6), until the [[Rice|rice]] is cooked and has absorbed the liquid.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a plain [[Salad|salad]] and [[Yoghurt|yogurt]] or with [[vegetables]].\n===Variations===\nIf liked, you can include some cooked [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]], in which case, reduce the amount of [[Rice|rice]].\n===Chef's notes===\nThe recipe may seem to require a rather large quantity of [[Rice|rice]], but you do need it.<BR>\nWhilst the mutton will be cooked at 1&frac14; hours it may still be a little tough, about 2 hours really did make the meat very tender.<BR>\nYou can also reduce the salt down to around 1tsp and it should still be nice, its a personal taste thing.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Kidreh (mutton with rice)]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes|Kidreh (mutton with rice)]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Kidreh (mutton with rice)]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Kidreh (mutton with rice)]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes|Kidreh (mutton with rice)]]\n[[Category:Mutton recipes|Kidreh (mutton with rice)]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes|Kidreh (mutton with rice)]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles|Kidreh (mutton with rice)]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#rice #mutton #butter #saffron #onion #stock #garlic #casseroledish #groundallspice #groundcinnamon #bayleaves </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

This is a Lebanese recipe, but similar versions are found in Turkey, Syria and Egypt.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| &#189; quantity of [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]], rolled into a circle and left to rise.\n| 1 x 400 g tin of chopped [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 1 lb [[Minced|minced]] [[Lamb|lamb]] (can be [[Frozen|frozen]] or fresh)\n| 1 large [[Spanish]] [[Onion|onion]], finely chopped\n| [[Olive oil]]\n| 1 bulb [[Roasted garlic|roasted garlic]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Lebanese za'atar spice mix recipe|Lebanese spice mix]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| 1-2 [[Chillies|chillies]], chopped\n| 1 tablespoon flat leaved [[Parsley|parsley]], finely chopped\n| 1 tablespoon [[Coriander|coriander]], finely chopped\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Mix the tinned [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] with the [[Lamb|lamb]] and drain through a [[Sieve|sieve]] and leave until you have a compact texture.\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 220\u00b0 C (425\u00b0 F - gas 7)\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]], add the [[Onion|onion]] and [[Fry|fry]] until soft.\n| Crush the [[Cloves|cloves]] of the [[Roast garlic|roast garlic]] lightly, using a spoon.\n| Mix all of the ingredients together.\n| When the circle of [[Pizza dough|pizza dough]] has doubled in height, spread the topping over it and [[Bake|bake]] for around 15-20 minutes.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nFine on its own or with [[Vegetables|vegetables]] or [[Salad|salad]].\n\n===Variations===\nAlthough not traditional, this recipe works well with [[Beef mince|beef mince]], rather then [[Lamb|lamb]].\n\n===Chef's notes===\nI used one [[Scotch bonnet|Scotch bonnet]] [[Chilli|chilli]] in this recipe, but you can use whichever sort you can get. Just cover with water and [[Simmer|simmer]], covered for 40 minutes.  Season with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n| In a separate large pan, heat the [[Butter|butter]] and when foaming, add the [[Caraway seeds|caraway seeds]] and saut\u00e9 for a minute\n| Add the [[Rice|rice]] and mix well to coat with [[Oil|oil]]\n| Mix in the [[Lamb|lamb]], its cooking juices, the [[Cabbage|cabbage]] and half the [[Parsley|parsley]]\n| Add enough water to just cover the [[Rice|rice]] by 1cm (&frac12;\")\n| Caver with a [[Cartouche|cartouche]] of [[greaseproof paper]] and a lid and heat for 8 minutes without stirring or fiddling with it\n| Take off the heat, remove the paper and leave to rest for 5 minutes, uncovered\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Lamb pilaf with cabbage and caraway cooking.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Before the cartouche\nImage:Lamb pilaf with cabbage and caraway ingredients.jpg|thumb|300px|right|The ingredients\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe sprinkled with the remaining [[Parsley|parsley]], spiced Yogurt, [[tomato salad]] and [[lemon wedges]]\n===Variations===\nI added a couple of sticks of finely chopped [[celery]] because I had some lying around. teaspoon [[Saffron|saffron]] powder \n| 500g shelled [[garden peas]] \n| 2 [[Tomatoes, peeled|tomatoes, peeled]] and chopped \n| 1 [[Belazu]] [[Preserved lemon|preserved lemon]] or more, cut into pieces \n| a dozen [[Green olives|green olives]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Put the [[Meat|meat]] in a large pot with the [[Oil|oil]], [[Onion|onion]], [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]], [[Ginger|ginger]] and [[Saffron|saffron]]. \n| Cover with water and cook, covered, for 1-1&frac12; hours until the [[Meat|meat]] is very tender, adding water to keep it covered in its [[Sauce|sauce]]. \n| Add the [[Peas|peas]], [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Preserved lemon|preserved lemon]] and [[Olives|olives]] and cook uncovered a few minutes longer, until the peas are tender and the [[Sauce|sauce]] reduced. Serve.\n}}\n(''Tamarind & Saffron by Claudia Roden'')\n\n\n{{Template:PeelingGinger}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Algerian recipes|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Belazu recipes|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Lamb recipes|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Libyan recipes|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Moroccan recipes|Tagine]]\n[[Category:North African recipes|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Tunisian recipes|Tagine]]\n[[Category:Stewed, braised or pot roasted]]\n{{Template:Belazu attribution}}\n\n\n===Belazu products used in this recipe===\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/belazu-pickled-lemons.html Belazu Preserved Lemon]\n* [http://www.mybelazu.com/details/rose-harissa.html Belazu Rose Harissa]\n==See also==\n{{Tagine-recipe-list}}\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#lambtagine #belazu #sauce #preservedlemon #ginger #onion #saffron #chillipowder #lamb #harissa #peas </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Lamb tagine with tomatoes and peas",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Lamb tagine with tomatoes and peas a meat recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#celery #lambshank #boiling #sherryvinegar #lambtaginewithtomatoesandpeas #garlic #simmer #saffron #oliveoil #onions #tomatoes \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Another slow-cooked lamb dish that has Middle Eastern origins\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1446\n|PortionCalories = 361\n|DatePublished=31st October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 2 hours 50 minutes\n |PrepTime = 20 minutes\n |CookTime =  2 hours 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Lamb tagine with tomatoes and pea recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Just made this - very nice.</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.6</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Made this last night - very nice!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Lamb tagine with tomatoes peas and aubergines.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Ready for a 2 hour simmer]]\nAnother slow-cooked [[Lamb|lamb]] dish that has Middle Eastern origins.  The original recipe was from one of the wonderful Moro books by Sam and Sam Clark, but as always, when it comes to cooking it, I use up bits and bobs found in the fridge and change it out of all recognition to the original recipe.\n\nThe fatty pork chop would '''never''' be in the original recipe which would be muslim in origin, however, it was spare in the fridge and adds a nice flavour to the oil\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 4 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 2 teaspoons white [[Cumin seeds|cumin seeds]] & 1 teaspoon [[black cumin seeds]], [[Ground|ground]] to  powder in a [[Coffee grinder|coffee grinder]] or [[Pestle and mortar|pestle and mortar]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[ras el hanout]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Paprika powder|paprika powder]]\n| 1 [[Chile de Arbole]] ground to powder or 1/2 a teaspoon of [[Chili powder|chili powder]]\n| 2 medium [[Onions|onions]], peeled and chopped\n| 4 cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| 1 large [[carrot]], peeled and cut into rings\n| 3 [[celery]] hearts with leaves, chopped into moons\n| 1 [[aubergine]], halved and sliced\n| 4 large [[Tomatoes, peeled|tomatoes, peeled]] and chopped\n| 1 [[Lamb shank]], on the bone\n| 1 large fatty [[pork chop]], cut into cubes \n| A splash of [[sherry vinegar]]\n| 1 650 ml cold water\n| 1 teaspoon [[Saffron strands|saffron strands]]. Stand in 2 tablespoons [[Boiling|boiling]] water for 15 minutes or more\n| 300 g [[Frozen peas|frozen peas]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* [[Skinning tomatoes|Rub the skins off]] the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] by [[Blanching|blanching]] water that has boiled and leave for 4 minutes.\n* Infuse the [[Saffron|saffron]] in 2 tablespoons of [[Boiling|boiling]] water for at least 15 minutes\n* Defrost the peas.\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a large pan, add the [[Olive oil|olive oil]], [[Onions|onions]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] and saut\u00e9 for 5 minutes until the onions have softened. Add the spices, stir-fry and then add the [[pork]] cubes and the [[lamb shank]] and stir-fry so the oil is flavoured with the spices and the meat is browned a little.\n| [[Deglaze]] the pan with a splash of [[sherry vinegar]]\n| Add the [[carrots]], [[celery]], [[aubergines]], [[tomatoes]], cold water and [[Saffron|saffron]] mix, bring to the [[Boil|boil]], reduce the heat and [[Simmer|simmer]] for 2 hours.\n| Add the [[Peas|peas]], remove the lid and [[Simmer|simmer]] for a further 25 minutes\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Couscous|couscous]] or crusty [[Bread|bread]]\n===Chef' note===\nDirectly from the pot it was quite liquid, which went very well with fresh bread, the next day though, the gravy had thickened up naturally. If you wanted a thicker sauce, just stir in a few teaspoons of cornflour, mixed with a tablespoon of water and heat for a few minutes whilst stirring.\n==See also==\n{{Tagine-recipe-list}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Lamb recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#celery #lambshank #boiling #sherryvinegar #lambtaginewithtomatoesandpeas #garlic #simmer #saffron #oliveoil #onions #tomatoes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

                "revisions": [

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Lebanese tomato soup, Vegetarian recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#butter #lebanesetomatosoup #onions #tomatoes #browned #cinnamon #fry #simmer #tomatopaste #panfried #boil \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=The idea for this soup came from a (translated) Lebanese cookbook I found in a second-hand bookshop\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 835\n|PortionCalories = 139\n|DatePublished=17th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 6\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 45 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Lebanese tomato soup recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Not Heinz \ud83c\udf45 soup</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.3</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Much nicer than Heinz \ud83c\udf45 soup! </span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nThe idea for this [[Soup|soup]] came from a (translated) Lebanese cookbook I found in a second-hand bookshop.  It is fairly basic but would make a good start for something more elaborate.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 7 oz [[Long grain rice|long grain rice]], washed\n| 2 oz chopped [[Onions|onions]]\n| 3 oz [[Butter|butter]]\n| 9 oz ripe [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], finely chopped\n| 2 tablespoons [[Salt|salt]]\n| 3 &frac12; [[Pints|pints]] cold water\n| 1 oz [[Tomato puree|tomato puree]]\n| [[Cinnamon]] powder for garnish\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Melt the [[Butter|butter]] and [[Fry|fry]] the [[Onions|onions]] until just [[Browned|browned]], about 5 minutes\n| In a large pot, add the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Rice|rice]], [[Salt|salt]] and water and bring to the [[Boil|boil]] over a fast heat\n| Add the [[Tomato paste|tomato paste]], [[Browned|browned]] [[Onions|onions]] and and remaining [[Butter|butter]]\n| Cover and [[Simmer|simmer]] for about 1 hour and 15 minutes\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe garnished with a little [[Cinnamon|cinnamon]] powder\n===Chef's notes===\nNowadays, 2 tablespoons of [[Salt|salt]] seems to be a little excessive.  I would suggest adding just a little and adjusting any seasoning at the end. You can add more but you can't take it away.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Lebanese recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#butter #lebanesetomatosoup #onions #tomatoes #browned #cinnamon #fry #simmer #tomatopaste #panfried #boil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Lebanese za'atar spice mix recipe",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Lebanese za'atar spice mix recipe Accompaniments\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#oliveoil #lebanesezaatarspicemixrecipe #sesameseeds #roasted #bake #vegetables #mortarandpestle #marjoram #yogurt #sumac #meats \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This version of Lebanese version of Za'atar contains sumac\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 171\n|PortionCalories = 17\n|DatePublished=29th May 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Servings: 10 - Makes 1 small pot - It will keep\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime = 10 minutes\n|PrepTime = 10 minutes\n|CookTime = None\n|Image = [[Image:Za'atar spice mixture.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Lovely over cauliflower</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">I especially like the flavour of the pine-nuts, an odd flavour in its own right.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:NonLoggedInUser|NonLoggedInUser]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis version of Lebanese version of [[Za'atar]] contains [[sumac]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 tablespoon ground [[sumac berries]]\n| 2 tablespoons dried [[thyme]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[roasted]] [[sesame seeds]]\n| 2 tablespoons  dried [[marjoram]]\n| 2 tablespoons  dried [[oregano]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[sea salt]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Combine everything except the [[sea salt]] and 1 tablespoon of [[roasted sesame seeds]]\n| Grind in a [[mortar and pestle]] or a [[coffee grinder]]\n| Mix in the [[sea salt]] and the remaining [[sesame seeds]]\n| Store in an airtight container, out of the light, for up to 2 months. It begins to lose its flavour if it'd stored any longer.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nIt can be used as a seasoning for [[meats]] and [[vegetables]]. \n\nMixed with [[olive oil]] it makes a spread called za'atar-wu-zayt as a dip for the sesame bread rings known as ka'ak.\n\nYou can spread it on a [[dough]] base and [[bake]] it as [[bread]], in which case it is called '''manaeesh bi zaatar'''. \n\nIt is often eaten as a breakfast snack, sprinkled on labneh ([[yogurt]] that has been drained until it becomes a tangy, creamy cheese).\n\n[[Za'atar]] is often sprinkled on [[hummus]] or served with [[olive oil]] as a spread or dip.\n\n==See also==\n\n* [[Za'atar spice mix recipe]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Za'atar]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Za'atar]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces|Za'atar]]\n[[Category:Marinades dressings and butters|Za'atar]]\n[[Category:Lebanese recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes|Za'atar]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Za'atar]]\n[[Category:Spices|Za'atar]]\n[[Category:Breakfast recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#oliveoil #lebanesezaatarspicemixrecipe #sesameseeds #roasted #bake #vegetables #mortarandpestle #marjoram #yogurt #sumac #meats </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Liver in sherry vinegar (Lebanese style)",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Liver in sherry vinegar (Lebanese style) a meat recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#liver #vinegar #cinnamonstick #garlic #mint #flour #ghee #sherryvinegar #lamb #fry #oliveoil \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=The inspiration for this recipe come from a translation of a 1960's Lebanese cook-book I picked up somewhere\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2164\n|PortionCalories = 541\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 45 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Liver in sherry vinegar (Lebanese style) recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Not as nice the second time around</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">3</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Maybe it was the liver, but quite tough</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Chef|Jerry]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Liver in sherry vinegar (Lebanese style).jpg|thumb|300px|right|Just before the vinegar is added. Note the huge cinnamon stick!]]\nThe inspiration for this recipe come from a translation of a 1960's Lebanese cook-book I picked up somewhere. I have always found [[Vinegar|vinegar]] a good accompaniment for [[Liver|liver]].  The original recipe just stated [[vinegar]], but I have changed this to [[Sherry vinegar|sherry vinegar]] because I love it so much.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 450 g [[Liver|liver]] ([[Lamb|lamb]] or [[Veal|veal]] preferred)\n| 1 scant teaspoon [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| [[Freshly ground black pepper]]\n| 1 [[Red bell pepper|red bell pepper]], de-seeded and sliced into strips\n| 3 fresh hot [[Chili peppers|chili peppers]], chopped into thin rings and de-seeded if you wish\n| 2.5 cm [[Cinnamon stick|cinnamon stick]], left whole, remove at end of cooking\n| 1 medium [[Onion|onion]], peeled and chopped finely\n| 5 [[Fat|fat]] [[Cloves|cloves]] of [[Garlic]], peeled and crushed mixed with &frac12; teaspoon [[Dried|dried]] [[Mint|mint]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Flour|flour]]\n| 50 ml [[Sherry vinegar|sherry vinegar]]\n| 50g [[Ghee|ghee]], [[Butter|butter]] or [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Wash and clean the [[Liver|liver]] and cut into thin slices.\n| Leave in a [[colander]] for 1 hour to drain excess liquid (if you have the time). Toss in the [[Flour|flour]] to coat\n| Melt the [[Ghee|ghee]] in a pan and [[Fry|fry]] the [[Red pepper|red pepper]] and [[Onions|onions]] until they start to [[Brown|brown]], then add the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Mint|mint]]. Just before the garlic starts to colour, tip in the [[Liver|liver]].\n| Add the [[Cinnamon stick|cinnamon stick]] and cook the [[Liver|liver]] for 10 minutes, turning often.\n| Add the [[Salt|salt]], [[Chillies|chillies]] and [[Vinegar|vinegar]], [[Deglaze|deglaze]] the pan, stir well and allow to reduce by a third\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe immediately, with [[cous-cous]] and vegetables.\n===Chef's note===\nThe recipe originally had 100 ml of [[vinegar]] but I found that too much for my taste so reduced it to 50ml.\n===Variations===\nUse [[red wine]] instead of [[vinegar]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Lamb recipes]]\n[[Category:Lebanese recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Offal recipes]]\n[[Category:Veal recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#liver #vinegar #cinnamonstick #garlic #mint #flour #ghee #sherryvinegar #lamb #fry #oliveoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

title": "Marinated olives",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Marinated olives, Spanish recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#olives #marinatedolives #sherryvinegar #marinate #greenolives #spices #chillipowder #blackolives #cuminseeds #garlic #olive \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Having realised that I was bored with pre-prepared stuffed olives, I decided to buy plain olives, complete with stones and marinate them\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1950\n|PortionCalories = 65\n|DatePublished=20th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Servings: 30 - Marinades 1.5 kg of olives\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 1 week\n |PrepTime = 1 week\n |CookTime = None\n |Image = [[Image:Olives in marinade.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Never thought of doing this</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Trouble is, can't find raw olives in bulk \ud83d\ude10</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\n \n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n\nHaving realised that I was bored with pre-prepared stuffed [[Olives|olives]], I decided to buy plain olives, complete with stones and [[Marinate|marinate]] them.  I happened to have a lot of olives when I made this, but you easily reduce the quantity.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 500 g [[Green olives|green olives]], stones intact\n| 1 kg [[Black olives|black olives]], stones intact\n| [[Olive oil]], to cover\n| 1 bulb or more of [[Garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| 1-2 teaspoons [[Chilli powder|chilli powder]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Cumin seeds|cumin seeds]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Dried thyme|dried thyme]] or [[Oregano|oregano]]\n| 90 ml [[Sherry vinegar|sherry vinegar]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Place the olives in an airtight container, such as a [[Lock&Lock boxes|Lock&Lock box]] and add enough olive oil to cover.\n| Stir in the remaining ingredients and shake vigorously.\n| Leave to [[Marinate|marinate]] for at least a week before consumption.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nUse with any recipe that calls for [[Olives|olives]], removing the stones if necessary.  Personally, I just enjoy pigging out on them on their own. \n===Variations===\nTry experimenting with your own choice of [[Herbs|herbs]] and [[Spices|spices]].  My green hojiblanca [[Olives|olives]] originated in the area around Fuente de Piedra in Andaluc\u00eda and the black ones were from Syria.  Use any combination of [[Olive|olive]] type, colour and origin.  Make your blend unique!\n===Chef's notes===\nIt is a good idea to shake the container several times daily as the [[Sherry vinegar|sherry vinegar]] sinks to the bottom.\n\nRemove the stones if you wish, but I find that [[Olives|olives]] taste better stoned at the last minute.\n\nDo not throw away the [[Marinade|marinade]] as it can be used as a dressing.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Olives marinated]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes|Olives marinated]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes|Olives marinated]]\n[[Category:North African recipes|Olives marinated]]\n[[Category:Pickles and preserves|Olives marinated]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Olives marinated]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Olives marinated]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Olives marinated]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Olives marinated]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Olives marinated]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#olives #marinatedolives #sherryvinegar #marinate #greenolives #spices #chillipowder #blackolives #cuminseeds #garlic #olive </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Mechouia",

This recipe is absolutely ideal for a barbecue\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 288\n|PortionCalories = 72\n|DatePublished=24th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Tunisian vegetable seller\n |Servings = 4 as a filling [[Side dish|side dish]]\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 30 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 15 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Mechouia recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Barbecue?</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.72</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Looks like a market to me</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis traditional Tunisian recipe combines [[Grilled|grilled]] [[Vegetables|vegetables]] and [[Hot chillies|hot chillies]] to make a delicious [[Salad|salad]].\n\nThis recipe is absolutely ideal for a [[Barbecue|barbecue]], espcially one with a hotplate\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 4 large [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] (plum-type preferred) [about 225 g]\n| 2 green [[Sweet peppers|sweet peppers]] [about 175 g]\n| 2 fresh [[Poblano chillies|poblano chillies]] [about 110 g]\n| 1 large [[Red onion|red onion]], un peeled\n| 2 large [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves, un peeled\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Caraway seeds|caraway seeds]], [[Ground|ground]] to a powder is a [[Coffee grinder|coffee grinder]]\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Coriander seeds|coriander seeds]], [[Ground|ground]] to a powder is a [[Coffee grinder|coffee grinder]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| [[Zest]] and [[Juice|juice]] from half a [[Lemon|lemon]]\n| 3 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 12 pitted [[Olives|olives]] (green or black) \n| 1 tablespoon [[Capers|capers]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Place the whole [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Sweet peppers|sweet peppers]], [[Chili peppers|chili peppers]], [[Onion|onion]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] on the [[Barbecue|barbecue]] hotplate, over the coals or even under an [[Oven|oven]] [[Grill|grill]].\n| Turn them often so they are really well charred.\n| Remove the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] as they are done, the [[Garlic|garlic]], for instance will be ready before the [[Onion|onion]].\n| Use the technique [[Roasted red pepper|shown here]], (or your own!), to skin the tomatoes, sweet and hot and peppers.  Remove the seeds and stems from the peppers\n| Remove the really burnt [[Onion|onion]] skin.\n| Cut all of the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] into nibble sized pieces an place in a large serving bowl.\n| Squish the [[Garlic|garlic]] from the [[Cloves|cloves]] with a cloth or a palette knife into a small bowl and mix with the garlic pulp.\n| Add the [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] and [[Zest|zest]] together with the [[Salt|salt]], [[Spices|spices]] and [[Olive oil|olive oil]].  Whisk the dressing and mix in with the [[Grilled|grilled]], chopped [[Vegetables|vegetables]].\n| Garnish with chopped [[Capers|capers]] and [[Olives|olives]]\n}}\n===Variations===\nUse [[Cumin seeds|cumin seeds]] instead of [[Caraway|caraway]] if [[caraway]] is not to your taste.\n\n[[Tuna|Tuna]] flaked into this salad, or sliced [[hard-boiled eggs]] would turn this into a main course.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Barbecue recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Tunisian recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#garlic #vegetables #grilled #mechouia #onion #zest #sweetpeppers #barbecue #tomatoes #oliveoil #ground </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Megadarra in a Squash",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Megadarra served in a Squash recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#rice #onions #lentils #squash #squashes #scoop #spices #orange #chillipowder #lemon #zest \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Pronounced mega-dah-ra, this simple Egyptian dish of rice, lentils and spiced onions is a super thing to squeeze into a squash\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1137\n|PortionCalories = 284\n|DatePublished=16th August 2014\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  50 minutes\n|PrepTime =  15 minutes\n|CookTime =  35 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Megadarra in a Squash recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Pretty picture</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">And a tasty meal that looks fun too.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nPronounced mega-dah-ra, this simple Egyptian dish of [[Rice|rice]], [[Lentils|lentils]] and spiced [[Onions|onions]] is a super thing to squeeze into a [[Squash|squash]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 4 mini or 1 medium-sized [[Squash|squash]]\n| 75g [[Brown basmati rice|brown basmati rice]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground pepper|freshly ground pepper]]\n| 1 mug of water\n| 400g tin of [[Lentils|lentils]]\n| 2 [[Onions|onions]], thinly sliced\n| 1 tablespoon [[Ground cumin|ground cumin]]\n| A pinch of [[Chilli powder|chilli powder]]\n| A pinch of [[Ground cinnamon|ground cinnamon]]\n| 1 [[Orange|orange]] or [[Lemon|lemon]]\n| 200g [[Natural yogurt|natural yogurt]] (optional)\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6), [fan [[Oven|oven]] 180\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Trim the base of your [[Squashes|squashes]] so they sit flat. Cut the top off your [[Squash|squash]] as if you were making a Hallowe\u0092en [[Pumpkin|pumpkin]].\n| [[Scoop]] out the [[Seeds|seeds]] (save them for later they are lovely [[Roasted|roasted]] with [[Sugar|sugar]], [[Salt|salt]] and [[Spice|spice]] till golden and crisp). Pop the [[Squash|squash]] on a [[Baking tray|baking tray]]. [[Roast]] for 30 mins or till completely tender.\n| Get a lidded pan hot for your [[Rice|rice]]. Toast for a mo. Add a pinch of [[Salt|salt]] and the water. Cover. Lower heat. [[Simmer]] for 20 mins.\n| Drain your [[Lentils|lentils]]. Rinse. Once the [[Rice|rice]] is done, drain it over the [[Lentils|lentils]]. Set aside.\n| Get a large [[Frying pan|frying pan]] hot. Add a gloss of [[Oil|oil]]. Tumble your [[Onions|onions]] and a good pinch of [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] in. Sizzle [[Onions|onions]] over medium heat for about 10 mins, till golden and a little crisp. Swirl in the [[Spices|spices]]. [[Scoop]] a spoonful of onions into a dish and set aside.\n| Keep the [[Onions|onions]] over medium heat. Fold the [[Rice|rice]] and [[Lentils|lentils]] in. Add a gloss of [[Oil|oil]]. Sizzle for a mo, to give the [[Rice|rice]] a little crispy edge to it.\n| Grate in the [[Zest|zest]] of the [[Orange|orange]] or [[Lemon|lemon]]. Add a good squeeze of [[Juice|juice]]. Taste. Season (and add more [[Spices|spices]]) as needed.\n| Once you're happy with the [[Rice|rice]], stuff it into the cooked and hollowed out [[Squashes|squashes]]. Scatter the reserved [[Onion|onion]] over the top.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a pot of [[Yogurt|yogurt]], dusted with a little [[Chilli powder|chilli powder]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Middle Eastern recipes]]\n[[Category:North African recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Squash recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Abel and Cole veg box recipes]]\n{{Template:Abel and Cole veg box recipes attribution}}\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#rice #onions #lentils #squash #squashes #scoop #spices #orange #chillipowder #lemon #zest </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
